       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/july/village_green_festival_book_signing_exhibition_and_djing">
         Village Green Festival: Book Signing, Exhibition and DJing
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        08 July 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 11:58
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.villagegreenfestival.com/">
          <img alt="Village Green Festival" height="721" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/49dbb4a0-2560-11e5-ab2a-aee5d44592c4" width="492"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         On Saturday 11th July Village Green Festival happens, This annual eventin Southend-on-Sea Essex has grown and grown over the years, it looks like it will be bigger and better than ever on Saturday.
        </p>
        <p>
         Curated by Arts body
         <a href="http://www.metalculture.com/">
          Metal
         </a>
         , Village Green is a rather special thing. Of course it is a great day out but it presents excellent art weihter it be sculpture, performance Music or indeed this year film and photography.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean will be exhibiting a number of large photographic print inChalkwell Hall it'san edit collection entitled
         <a href="http://www.villagegreenfestival.com/lineup/detail/dean-chalkley-.html">
          SONICS
         </a>
         ,coupled to this is theYoung Souls film andtwo wall take over fromReturn of the Rudeboy.
        </p>
        <p>
         As you'll be aware of Dean and Harris are theauthors of the
         <a href="http://www.villagegreenfestival.com/lineup/detail/dean-chalkley.html">
          Return of the Rudeboybook,
         </a>
         it will be available to buy and there'll be a personal book signing too, likely to be 2pm (This may change though, exact time TBC on the 11-7-15)
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean will also join Scully Evans to Dj asthe duo become the
         <a href="http://www.villagegreenfestival.com/lineup/detail/black-cat.html">
          Black Cat Dj's
         </a>
         playing at certain times through out the day on the Riverside stage. They will be inposition and playing some Ska and Rudeboy soundsbefore
         <a href="http://theselecter.net/">
          The Selecte
         </a>
         r
         <a href="http://www.villagegreenfestival.com/lineup/detail/the-selecter.html">
          later in the afternoon
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         So come to the festival it is great value and a great day out.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">

         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/june/prinzhorn_dance_school_reign_film">
         Prinzhorn Dance School : REIGN Film
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        09 June 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:08
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=G7FpZZFLO5s">
          <img alt="prinzhorn dance school film for Reign" height="384" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/8483ea90-0e91-11e5-a39e-92ce347ad47a" width="721"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Today
         <a href="http://www.prinzhorn-dance-school.com/prinzhorn/">
          Prinzhorn Dance School
         </a>
         release their new album Home Economics (
         <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/album/home-economics/id981682536">
          itunes
         </a>
         <a href="http://www.roughtrade.com/events/2015/6/1346">
          rough trade
         </a>
         ), an amazing piece of work.This collection of 6 haunting tracks arelike Bauhaus Brainworms enteringyour head and never leaving. Home Economics is certainly not throw away music, unusual structures make you want to listen more and more. Click on the image above to see the film that Dean has made for the lead track 'REIGN' this song has already broken out of any confinement, it is all over
         <a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/programmes/b05sdnc5">
          6music
         </a>
         and now
         <a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/programmes/b05vcyj3">
          radio1
         </a>
         . ('
         <a href="http://www.shitrobot.com/">
          Shit Robot
         </a>
         ' fellow
         <a href="http://dfarecords.com/">
          DFA
         </a>
         label mate has done a remix of the track that is now reaching out into more club scenes..)
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean also photographed Prinzhorn Dance School for the album cover and press imagery. Final cover artwork was a collaboration between the band and Dean, beautifully screen printed and worked on by Tobin Prinz.
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2015/june/prinzhorn_dance_school_reign_film#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2015/june/prinzhorn_dance_school_reign_film">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/june/rudeboy_salon_5th_and_6th_june_plus_private_view_on_the_4th">
         Rudeboy Salon : 5th &amp; 6th June plus private view on the 4th
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        07 June 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:23
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="rudeboy salon" height="640" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/d6e0b174-0d42-11e5-8228-92ce347ad47a" width="640"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="https://instagram.com/returnoftherudeboy/">
          Rudeboy Salon
         </a>
         was a great success. The environment of the
         <a href="http://www.thehospitalclub.com/">
          Hospital Club
         </a>
         was a perfect place tounveilthe latest chapter in the journey of this ever evolving landmark show.
        </p>
        <p>
         From the moment the doors opened to the private view on the evening of Thursday 4th June it was clear this happening was going to be a memorable occasion.
        </p>
        <p>
         Initiallythis event was to herald the release of the first UK version of the self-titled Return of the Rudeboy Book.
        </p>
        <p>
         (There will be a post tomorrow on the blog dedicated to the book and how you can order your copy)
        </p>
        <p>
         But the whole event once again became an inspirational moment
        </p>
        <p>
         On the evening of the 5th June there was a 'Conversation - Q&amp;A ' between
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norman_Jay">
          Norman Jay MBE
         </a>
         and Stephanie from
         <a href="http://www.letsbebrief.co.uk/">
          LBB
         </a>
         . This was afascinatingand enlightening moment that touchedon Normans history musical inspiration , going to New York and discovering new music and returning to the UK and steadfastly presenting it to crowds and even in light of some elements of the audience pelting him with objects he stood to his belief. He explained about getting the Good Times carnival plot and howonce again, against the odds he overcame manyobstacles...His political background and his view of the future were also discussion topics, lots of interesting things came up and some funny ones tooincluding the reason for Normans Hat love stemming from the hot summer of 1976 and its swarms of ladybirds that had the habit of gettingpresencein his afro.. 'Lifeand (Good) Times' indeed it was...
        </p>
        <p>
         At 3pm in the afternoon of Saturday6th June, Drummer Producer andmemberof The Specials
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Bradbury_%28drummer%29">
          John 'Brad' Bradbury
         </a>
         talked with Stephanie LBB for over an hour infront of the audience.This was a very rare moment as Brad does not give interviews, he explained that he never really likes doing them so he chooses not to agree to partake but for Return of the Rudeboy and inthe dynamic it creates he did agreed. Well, what a brilliant conversation it was... Bradtalked aboutgrowingup in Coventry, hisviewson life and missionthrough music to bring anethos to the audience. Brad illuminated what it was like to be in The Specials and talked over how the band functioned and still to this day moves on, it didn't stop there was so many aspects talked about..but if you were there you will know...
        </p>
        <p>
         Brad and Norman were very charismatic and a both gave incredibleinsightsinto their lives that are never releasedunder differentcircumstances so it was a realprivilegeto beinthecompanyof these guys and hear what they had to say.
        </p>
        <p>
         Stephanie navigated the conversations effortlessly and please look out for
         <a href="http://www.letsbebrief.co.uk/">
          LBB
         </a>
         as they are a vital and important organisation thatpositivelybrings knowledge to people.
        </p>
        <p>
         The above pictureis a detail of the new 'Rudeboy Sound System' it has never been seen before the Rudeboy Salon.
        </p>
        <p>
         Acollaborationbetween -Return of the Rudeboy x Andrew Ibi x Goomans
        </p>
        <p>
         The installation curated by Dean and Harris comprises of 90 Goodmans individualHeritageRadios stacked together in a Sound System Box Rig andthen customisedandappropriatedby artist Andrew Ibe. Many of the illustrations refer to musical influences of Rudeboys in times past as well as Dean and Harris's 10 Favourite Rudeboy tracks.
        </p>
        <p>
         Throughout the period of the Rudeboy Salon many Djs played in the Gallery including :
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Justin_Robertson">
          Justin Roberson
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/4hero">
          Dego (4 Hero)
         </a>
         ,Ramrock Hi-Fi (
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ashley_Beedle">
          Ashley Beedle
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://www.juno.co.uk/products/ramrock-allstars-return-of-the-gentleman-rudeboy/542963-01/">
          Jo Wallace
         </a>
         ),
         <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=oeWKm2nT6ME">
          Mark Professor
         </a>
         (Wreck it up) ,John Kelly,
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/neil.barker.7583?fref=ts">
          Neil Barker
         </a>
         (Black Cat) , Andrew Ibi (artist and '
         <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=V1I11lE9BtY">
          Reference Library
         </a>
         ' dj of course),
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Debbie_Smith_%28musician%29">
          Debbie Smith
         </a>
         (Nitty Gritty)
        </p>
        <p>
         Many visitors came to the gallery and enjoyed the edit version of the Return of the Rudeboy exhibition.The book wasexclusivelyon sale at the event and is now in their hands .. it has beenreceivedwell.
        </p>
        <p>
         You can order your copy on line by clicking
         <a href="http://www.returnoftherudeboy.com/">
          here
         </a>
         and following the link.
        </p>
        <p>
         The Rudeboy Salon was supported by
         <a href="http://www.goodmans.co.uk/blog-rudeboy-salon.html">
          Goodmans
         </a>
         the sound company and what great support it was to enable this event to happen the way that Dean and Harris wanted it to.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/may/return_of_the_rudeboy_book_launch_event_rudeboy_salon_5th_and_6th_june_2015">
         Return of the Rudeboy Book Launch event : Rudeboy Salon  5th and 6th June 2015
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        27 May 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:03
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="Reudeboy Salon" height="721" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/5e06fbb2-043e-11e5-b64c-46bfd53c547e" width="589"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Hold Tight!!
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.returnoftherudeboy.com/">
          Return of the Rudeboy
         </a>
         is releasing a book ahard cover128pg beautifully printed companion to the Return of the Rudeboy exhibition.
        </p>
        <p>
         The launch event for the book is called the'Rudeboy Salon'. Thistwo day event taking place on the 5th and 6th June 2015.
        </p>
        <p>
         The Rudeboy Salon reclaims the notion of the old school art and cultural happening itwill be a happening in keeping with the Return of the Rudeboy styleandtakes place at the
         <a href="http://www.thehospitalclub.com/">
          Hospital Club
         </a>
         Gallery, Ground Floor,Endell Street Covent Garden.
        </p>
        <p>
         The book will be exclusively available to purchase in the 'Rudeboy Salon' over those two days, there after it will be available at selective outlets and on-line (details of this will be in a later post)
        </p>
        <p>
         Free entry and open to the public from 10am - 10pm .
        </p>
        <p>
         As illustrated in the events schedule Dean and Harris will be attending and taking part ina number of book signings, there will be djs throughout the days/evenings and also Rudeboy Salon Talks with special guest Q&amp;A's  (To be announced...so watch this space seats will be limited so be poised)
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="https://instagram.com/returnoftherudeboy/">
          here
         </a>
         is a link to the Return of the Rudeboy instagram too...nice!
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/may/paul_weller_for_the_observer_magazine">
         Paul Weller for The Observer Magazine
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        12 May 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:42
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="Paul Weller" height="721" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/47adc5a8-f8a4-11e4-afda-7ad1c200b233" width="721"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Sunday's feature about
         <a href="http://paulweller.com/">
          Paul Weller
         </a>
         has attracted a lot of interest. Often known as the Mod Father, Paul Weller discussed his current attitudes, politics, family life and mindset together with his deep passion for music and the direction it is taking him. You can read the article written by
         <a href="http://www.mirandasawyer.com/">
          Miranda Sawyer
         </a>
         <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/music/2015/may/10/paul-weller-miss-the-chaos-and-madness">
          here
         </a>
         . Dean explained that this was a significant shoot for many reasons not least that Paul isa person that has influenced hisperspective on life and taste both musically andin a fashion context. Paul'ssteadfast attitude sets him out from others. This isthe 5th time Dean has photographed Paul Weller each time has been a total pleasure according to Mr.Chalkley.
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/may/young_souls_at_the_vortigern_gallery_margate_22515_until_26615">
         Young Souls at the Vortigern Gallery Margate 22-5-15 until 26-6-15
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        12 May 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:56
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.vortigernmargate.com/">
          <img alt="Vortigern exhibition poster" height="721" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/f224c916-f89d-11e4-b0a5-46bfd53c547e" width="511"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Young Souls project arose when Dean was invited to submit photographic essay and a short film to 125 Magazine, the publication always revolves around a word and in this instance it was theinterpretation of Religion. Deanexplains Immediately the phase Keep the faith came into my head, music never being far from my mind, I thought that this would be a great opportunity to explore and present a subject that is close to my heart. With the stills I didnt want to recreate the past, but I did aim to produce timeless works that illustrate the culture as never before."
        </p>
        <p>
         For those of you who know about the culture of Northern Soul you will not need any explaination however for those new to this fabulous scene you can start off by having a look at the wiki link
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_soul">
          here
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         Vortigern Margate is a new photographic gallery and rare bookshop based in the Old Town of Margate in Kent, England.Itrepresents a wide range of photographic artists andalso stocksa carefully curated selection of mostly first edition rare and out of print photo-books and vintage magazines from the 1950's to the present day.
        </p>
        <p>
         Vortigern Margate takes it's name from Margate's famous Vortigern caves and is the premiere destination in the south east of England for photographers and those who love the medium.
        </p>
        <p>
         In the past Dean was invited to screenhis award winning short film
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/video/">
          Young Souls
         </a>
         at the
         <a href="https://www.turnercontemporary.org/">
          Turner Contemporary Gallery
         </a>
         so it is fitting that now Dean will present a selected edit of the original Young Souls exhibition in the Vortigern Gallery afine new gallery also in Margate.
        </p>
        <p>
         Vortigern opensThursdays  Sundays 11am- 5pm click on the poster to link to the galleries website.
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2015/may/young_souls_at_the_vortigern_gallery_margate_22515_until_26615#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2015/may/young_souls_at_the_vortigern_gallery_margate_22515_until_26615">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/april/russell_brand_the_emperors_new_clothes_poster">
         Russell Brand : The Emperor's New Clothes : Poster
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        21 April 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:27
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://studiocanaltickets.co.uk/gb/the-emperors-new-clothes/?campaign=GSearch">
          <img alt="russell brand film" height="480" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/c0e18c56-e7f7-11e4-9237-46bfd53c547e" width="721"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Tonight
         <a href="https://twitter.com/rustyrockets">
          Russell Brands
         </a>
         film 'The Emperor's New Clothes', is releaved...Directed by
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Winterbottom">
          Michael Winterbottom
         </a>
         it's an incisive look at the system and structure of our society.Using a mixture of documentary, interviews, archive footage and comedy, Russell will takeus from his hometown Grays in Essex, to the heart of London City and on to the Big Apple. This daring film aims toshake up the world.The film will have an impact and it will be very interesting to see the ripple and effect...Click
         <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.co.uk/2015/03/30/russell-brand-the-emperors-new-clothes-trailer_n_6967282.html">
          here
         </a>
         for the a sneak at the trailer.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean photographed Russell for the poster and related press.
        </p>
        <p>
         For news of screenings click
         <a href="https://www.google.co.uk/movies?hl=en&amp;near=London,+UK&amp;dq=the+emperors+new+clothes+film&amp;sort=1&amp;mid=143f68284d242708&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=Xv81Vc-tIILjaoCvgfAO&amp;ved=0CDUQwAMoDw">
          here
         </a>
        </p>

       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        20 April 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  4:33
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/film/2015/apr/19/timothy-spall-dealing-with-ghosts-the-enfield-haunting">
          <img alt="Timothy Spall" height="544" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/7c95765a-e772-11e4-9a44-7ad1c200b233" width="396"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         This feature is fascinating, written by
         <a href="http://www.elizabethdayonline.co.uk/">
          Elizabeth Day
         </a>
         it transports you into the world of Timothy, reading it you get to understand how he is, his mannerisms and sense of humour too. Timothy is a genius there is no doubt , but he is also a person who tells it like it is who brain is razor sharp and expansive. He has had many ups and downs and serious illness as wellbut through it all shines a brilliant man who's craft as an actor penetrates deeply into our psyche. You can read more by visiting the Observers web page simply click
         <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/film/2015/apr/19/timothy-spall-dealing-with-ghosts-the-enfield-haunting">
          here
         </a>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/march/heroes_vortigern_gallery_margate">
         Heroes : Vortigern Gallery Margate
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        29 March 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:02
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="vortigernmargate.com" height="721" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/72f125fe-d60b-11e4-b405-0e87424f6ea9" width="511"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean, Rankin, Jamie Beeden, Pat Pope , Scarlet Page, Mark Blower, Joe Dilworth and Tim Kent are collectively exhibiting photographic works at Margate's Contemporary Photography Gallery
         <a href="http://www.vortigernmargate.com/">
          Vortigern
         </a>
         . The group show entitled ' Heroes' celebrates the concept of the photographer photographing their
         <em>
          Hero.
         </em>
         This novel concept has brought together some of the most prolific photographers who often work within the realm of 'music'. The exhibition actually opens on the 3rd but as there is a Bank Holiday it is a perfect opportunity to make alaunchevent on the Saturday (4th) to enable those travelling to the coast to enjoy the moment..all are welcome. Following this launch event there will be a special club night "STUDIO 45 vs BLACK CAT' at the Westcoast in King Street where Dean will join Dean Thatcher Stephen Saunders and Neil Barker to play Northern Soul, Ska and other uptight Dance floor tunes. It will be in a way an aftershow party for the Gallery event as well as a Bank Holiday outing for Studio 45 vs Black Cat. See the facebook event
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/events/393565334159217/">
          https://www.facebook.com/events/393565334159217/
         </a>
         ...and see you there
        </p>
       </div>

         Return of the Rudeboy : Tokyo Poster
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        11 March 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:40
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="return of the rudeboy Tokyo poster" height="719" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/d22d4cb8-c82e-11e4-8054-0e87424f6ea9" width="509"/>

       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2015/march/return_of_the_rudeboy_tokyo_poster#comments">

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/march/return_of_the_rudeboy_tokyo_japan_20th26th_march_laforet">
         Return of the Rudeboy : Tokyo : Japan : 20th-26th March : Laforet
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        09 March 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:30
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.returnoftherudeboy.jp/" title="Return of the Rudeboy Tokyo Japan">
          <img alt="Return of the Rudeboy : Japan: Tokyo" height="426" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/69a295e6-c5f3-11e4-bc88-0e87424f6ea9" width="721"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Following the success of Return of the Rudeboy at Somerset House the Rudeboys are on the move andwill now land in Tokyo Japan. Dean and Harris always said that the work was going to be dynamic and this latest chapter underlines that fact.
        </p>
        <p>
         Taking place on the gigantic top gallery level ofLaForet in the Harajuku District Return of the Rudeboy is certainly creating a great anticipation and is set to explode into peoples consciousnessas soon as it begins.
        </p>
        <p>
         Theshow runs from 20th March until 24th March click on the image to go to The Japanese Return of the Rudeboy website.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean and Harris will be making a number of appearances in the gallery and at special related events in Tokyo through the run of the show, speaking and also Djing.
        </p>
        <p>
         More on this later, it will be a rolling news story...keep it locked and if you are in Tokyo or know anyone who is tell them to get along to this important ground breaking exhibition.
        </p>
       </div>

        </a>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2015/february/field_project_brighton_calling_all_makers">
         Field Project: Brighton: Calling all Makers
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        11 February 15
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  2:40
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://fieldbtn.com/" title="feild propject link">
          <img alt="Field Project Brighton" height="572" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/dfbd682a-b1fb-11e4-9229-f6927ae6a2e0" width="461"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Just unveiled; a series of gigantic close up photographic portraits shot by Dean for the Field Project in Brighton.
        </p>
        <p>
         To introduce the project here is what the organiserssay:
        </p>
        <p>
         '
         <em>
          We want to work with you; Brightons makers, creatives and innovators, to transform a corner of Brighton into something more than just a field. The possibilities are endless. A field of inquiry, of knowledge, of expertise, of endeavour. A playing field. A field of innovation.
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <em>
          Over the coming months we will be inviting you to hold events, exhibitions and providing opportunities for you to shape what FIELD should be.
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <em>
          You all have something in common: you make. We are inviting you to make FIELD your home for now and the future. Your activities will define what will in time become an exciting new community. The ideas generated by FIELD will inform, shape and deliver the future of the maker community at the gateway of the city of Brighton.
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <em>
          For now, sign up to FIELD and well be in touch very soon.'
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         So just visit
         <a href="http://fieldbtn.com/">
          http://fieldbtn.com/
         </a>
         to go to the Field Projects website and get involved.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         If you are in or near Brighton it is worth keep an eye on thelocationas it will be changing as the months roll by.
        </p>
        <p>
         This and other large images from the series are situated opposite the University, the official addressis :
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Preston Barracks, University of Brighton, Lewes Rd, Brighton BN2 4GL
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2015/february/field_project_brighton_calling_all_makers#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2015/february/field_project_brighton_calling_all_makers">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/december/the_arena_now_viewable_on_vimeo">
         The Arena: Now Viewable on Vimeo
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        30 December 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  7:56
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="https://vimeo.com/111724483">
          <img alt="The Arena Film Blog Poster" height="395" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/e3f09d14-905d-11e4-b3e0-0e72c8382c78" width="721"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p class="first">
         View Deansshort film 'The Arena' on Vimeo now. Find a calm place, if you are watching on a computer put your headphones on, Turn up the volume and prepare for an emotional journey. The film has been screened at theV&amp;A Museum as part of the special 'Friday Lates' New British take over and at the Southend Film Festival where it was the opening feature of the closing Gala.
        </p>
        <p class="first">
         Filmed at the Spedeworth Motorsports Aldershot Raceway Arena.
        </p>
        <p>
         This film features on The New British LEGACY iPad App, along with 12 other short films. There is also an exclusive photographic reportage shot by Dean at 'Arena Essex' and a written essay too . The Combination of thesestudies make getting the App a must!..
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Get your copy of the App by following the link below: (Available for Ipads only)
        </p>
        <p>
         <br/>
         <a href="http://appstore.com/thenewbritish/thenewbritish" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          appstore.com/thenewbritish/thenewbritish
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/december/the_new_british_legacy_edition_now_live_for_ipads">
         The New British : Legacy Edition Now Live for Ipads
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        17 December 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:46
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="the new british launch party: 4th Dec" height="258" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/f0ae3784-71ac-11e4-8769-9ee170532087" width="721"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p style="margin: .1pt 0cm .1pt 0cm;">
         <span style="font-size: 13.5pt; font-family: Verdana; color: black;">
          A couple of weeks ago Dean joined
          <a href="http://thenewbritish.com/">
           Kez Glozier
          </a>
          Editor and several New British contributors on a panel discussion at the
          <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheNewBritishMag?sk=wall">
           Apple Store
          </a>
          in Londons Regent Street. The discussion hosted by
          <a href="http://www.letsbebrief.co.uk/about/">
           LBB 'sStephanie McLaren-Neckles's
          </a>
          delved into the world of the New British and explored what makes itone ofthe most if not the most vital and exciting publication to emerge in recent years.
         </span>
        </p>
        <p style="margin: .1pt 0cm .1pt 0cm;">
        </p>
        <p style="margin: .1pt 0cm .1pt 0cm;">
         Well Legacy is now out, only available for Ipads this new issue is sensational!
        </p>
        <p>
         Watch a special trailer to the App:
        </p>
        <p class="p2">
         <span class="s1">
          <a href="https://vimeo.com/114270029">
           https://vimeo.com/114270029
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="p3">
         Watch a showreel featuring the 12 short films that are on the App.
        </p>
        <p class="p2">
         <span class="s1">
          <a href="https://vimeo.com/114601627">
           https://vimeo.com/114601627
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="p1">
         Heres the link for iTunes for the App, a must see must get involved with:
        </p>
        <p class="p2">
         <a href="http://appstore.com/thenewbritish/thenewbritish">
          appstore.com/thenewbritish/thenewbritish
         </a>
        </p>
        <p class="p2">
        </p>
        <p class="p2">

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/november/the_new_british_legacy_edition_launch_4th_december">
         The New British : Legacy Edition Launch :4th December
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        21 November 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  6:34
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/events/604150883024046/?ref=3&amp;ref_newsfeed_story_type=regular">
          <img alt="the new british launch party: 4th Dec" height="258" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/f0ae3784-71ac-11e4-8769-9ee170532087" width="721"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://thenewbritish.com/">
          The New British
         </a>
         is something special, brainchild of Kez Glozier in association with
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Neville_Brody">
          Neville Brody
         </a>
         it celebrates all of contemporary British culture in a way no other publication does. Dean is a big supporter of TNB and had work in 'Issue Zero' alongside contributors includingNick Knight and Magnum Photographers.
        </p>
        <p>
         The Publication has now become an App and with a revolutionary design, Issue Zero can be downloaded
         <a href="http://thenewbritish.com/">
          here
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Such is the impact of TNB
         <a href="https://www.apple.com/uk/retail/regentstreet/">
          Apple
         </a>
         are hosting the launch of the forthcomingissue "Legacy" at the Apple Store in Regent Street London. on the 4th December 2014.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean has contributed a large project to this new issue and is really excited to see it go live. Comprising of a photgraphic essay and a film ...very exciting indeed!!!!
        </p>
        <p>
         TNB is a vital and extraordinary thing, and this is further inforces (not that it really needs to be) the fact that TNB is where it's at .
        </p>
        <p>
         You can come to the Launch by following the link to The New British's Facebook page have a look and then email
         <a href="mailto:join@thenewbritish.com">
          join@thenewbritish.com
         </a>
         with your full names, be part of this do not miss out.
        </p>
        <p>
         LEGACY is launching at the
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Apple-Store/284206318273275">
          Apple Store
         </a>
         (Regent's Street).
        </p>
        <p>
         VIP after party at
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheScotchOfStJames">
          The Scotch Of St James
         </a>
         (with special live performances)
        </p>
        <p>
         More details coming soon. On
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheNewBritishMag">
          The New British
         </a>
         site
        </p>
        <p>
         Here is the Facebook link in full to share:
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/events/604150883024046/?ref=3&amp;ref_newsfeed_story_type=regular">
          https://www.facebook.com/events/604150883024046/?ref=3&amp;ref_newsfeed_story_type=regular
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2014/november/the_new_british_legacy_edition_launch_4th_december#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2014/november/the_new_british_legacy_edition_launch_4th_december">
         </fb:comments-count>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/november/russell_brand_revolution">
         Russell Brand : Revolution
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        06 November 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  6:55
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="russell brand" height="721" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/04dcd338-65e5-11e4-81f8-226c7ced4085" width="468"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Russell Brand is certainly stirring up an exciting political discussion. REVOLUTION (sorry couldn't turn the Eround)is Russell's latest book and deals with the notion of the structure of our society, freedom and alternative thinking but delivered with his usual sharp and unique manner . The book has been met with an explosion of activity,with the backdrop of the overall political climate it is perfectly timed.
        </p>
        <p>
         This inescapable image was shot by Dean in London.REVOLUTIONis a National best seller you will be able to buy it at your local
         <a href="http://localbookshops.tbphost.co.uk/tbp.web/customeraccesscontrol/home.aspx?d=localbookshops&amp;s=C&amp;r=10000020&amp;ui=0&amp;bc=0">
          book shop
         </a>
         ... Please support you local book shops as they are important things to keep aliveandmust not be lost.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">

         Screen Social: Northern Soul Stew Event
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        05 October 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  2:14
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="Screen Social Poster 8th October" height="719" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/7c526e18-4c91-11e4-8d3a-226c7ced4085" width="509"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Cannes in a Van + Swhype presentSCREEN SOCIAL: NORTHERN SOUL STEW
        </p>
        <p>
         OnWednesday 8th October
         <strong>
         </strong>
         Screen Socia
         <strong>
          l
         </strong>
         arehosting another charity
         <em>
          event
         </em>
         in London Northern Soul Stew
         <strong>
          .
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         With a nod to the release of British feature film -
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/northernsoulthefilm">
          Northern Soul,
         </a>
         the music vs film night is back at The Book Clubin Londons Shoreditch for a night of floor fillers, films and foolery.
        </p>
        <p>
         Mixing up the soul soup with their 45s will be guest DJs Sonny Scully Evans (main guy in Young Souls) and Dean
         <strong>
          ,
         </strong>
         there will be a live performance by
         <strong>
         </strong>
         vocal trio
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JETmusicUK?utm_source=Swhype+%2F+CIAV+%2F+Screen+Social&amp;utm_campaign=b63be826e4-Screen_Social_24_09_14-opened_recent_campaigns&amp;utm_medium=email&amp;utm_term=0_f17d44ebf7-b63be826e4-306461169">
          <span class="s1">
           J.E.T
          </span>
         </a>
         <strong>
         </strong>
         playing their own brand of soul, and a host of films, from independent directors to YouTube sensations and everything in between. Sounds like a great night ahead.
        </p>
        <p>
         Please register online if you can to let the organisers knowyoure coming click
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/events/348806578617999/">
          here
         </a>
         for theScreen SocialFacebook page
        </p>
        <p>
         All proceeds from this Screen Social go to the housing &amp; homelessness charity
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/ShelterUK?utm_source=Swhype+%2F+CIAV+%2F+Screen+Social&amp;utm_campaign=b63be826e4-Screen_Social_24_09_14-opened_recent_campaigns&amp;utm_medium=email&amp;utm_term=0_f17d44ebf7-b63be826e4-306461169">
          Shelter
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p class="p1">
         If you register online theorganisers
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/swhype?utm_source=Swhype+%2F+CIAV+%2F+Screen+Social&amp;utm_campaign=b63be826e4-Screen_Social_24_09_14-opened_recent_campaigns&amp;utm_medium=email&amp;utm_term=0_f17d44ebf7-b63be826e4-306461169">
          <span class="s1">
           Swhype
          </span>
         </a>
         will donate an extra 1 to the charity.
        </p>
        <p>
         This will be a night full of music, film, chat and drinks so make it down onWednesday 8th OctobertoThe Book Club, 100 Leonard St,London EC2A 4RH,7pm  12pm | 4 / 3 online
        </p>
        <p>
         All proceeds will go to the housing &amp; homelessness charity Shelter
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/august/the_original_rude_boy_book_reading_with_neville_staple">
         The Original Rude Boy: Book reading with Neville Staple
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        20 August 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:00
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <h3>
         Friday 22 August
        </h3>
        <h3>
         16:00
         <br/>
         <a href="http://www.somersethouse.org.uk/visual-arts/return-of-the-rudeboy" target="_blank">
          Limited spaces, sign up in the gallery from 15:30
         </a>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         Join us as musician and former vocalist of The Specials Neville Staple comes to visit the exhibition in its final week. Together with his wife Christine, Neville will be reading extracts from his autobiography, The Original Rude Boy. As witty, incisive and entertaining as the man himself the book encompasses early life in Coventry and his involvement in the Two Tone movement in the 70s and 80s. In between readings our guests will be reflecting upon the cultural, social and political landscape at the time. Neville will also be signing copies of The Original Rude Boy in the bookshop after the reading.
        </h3>
        <p>
         <img alt="neville staple" height="721" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/d3d92516-2791-11e4-ba42-0a6b09a68d06" width="471"/>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/august/new_york_times_return_of_the_rudeboy">
         New York Times : Return of the Rudeboy
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        05 August 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:46
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="dean and harris" height="544" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/5d968a4c-1c8d-11e4-b62f-0a6b09a68d06" style="undefined" width="721"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Today The New York Times has printed a feature on Return of the Rudeboy. Click
         <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/2014/08/05/arts/international/britains-rudeboys-ride-again.html">
          here
         </a>
         to read the on-line version of the article.
        </p>
        <p>
         Above is the picture that accompanies the feature taken by
         <a href="http://blog.gettyimages.com/author/peter-macdiarmid/">
          Peter Macdiarmid
         </a>
         in
         <a href="http://www.somersethouse.org.uk/visual-arts/return-of-the-rudeboy">
          Somerset House
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         The New York Times feature is a significant moment for the exhibition, international interest has been flooding through, this coupled with the news that over 42,000 people have visited the show so far (With three weeks still remaining closing date 25th August 2014). It clearly illustrates that Return of the Rudeboy has struck a chord in a UK and global sense.
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/july/lets_be_brief_talk_with_dean_and_harris_announced_03_august_2014">
         Let's Be Brief : Talk with Dean and Harris announced : 03 AUGUST 2014
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        19 July 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  6:43
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.letsbebrief.co.uk/return-of-the-rudeboy/">
          <img alt="LBB Talk" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/b1b76292-0f6b-11e4-ad7b-0a6b09a68d06"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         As they say:
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          SUNDAY 03 AUGUST 2014 // 1:30-3:30 // 10 // OVAL SPACE29-32 THE OVAL, HACKNEY, LONDON,E2 9DT
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         If you were to prise apart the heart of many cultural zeitgeist, youd most likely find design, music and fashion as integral components.
        </p>
        <p>
         Theres not always a logical and linear reason for why trends appear, but it is why culture remains such an interesting phenomena.
        </p>
        <p>
         In collaboration with Fashion Sunday, LBB will host a live interview with fashion-industry favourite, creative director /
         <a href="http://www.hbyharris.com/">
          H by Harris
         </a>
         founder Harris Elliott and prolific photographer / filmmaker for musics most wanted photographer
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
          Dean Chalkley
         </a>
          both cultural instigators in their own right.
        </p>
        <p>
         The topic of conversation will be the pairs recent visual arts collaboration:
         <a href="http://www.somersethouse.org.uk/visual-arts/return-of-the-rudeboy">
          The Return of the Rudeboy
         </a>
         , currently exhibiting at Somerset House. The multimedia exhibition featuring photography, installation and events, showcases the sartorial subculture of the 21st century Rudeboy as well as the contributing culture that underpins the movement. From its roots of 50s Kingston, Jamaica, 80s Two-tone Britain to the contemporary take on Rudie style.
        </p>
        <p>
         LBB is a great site check out their stuff
         <a href="http://www.letsbebrief.co.uk">
          here
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2014/july/lets_be_brief_talk_with_dean_and_harris_announced_03_august_2014#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2014/july/lets_be_brief_talk_with_dean_and_harris_announced_03_august_2014">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

         <br/>

        <p>
         <a href="http://www.channel4.com/news/return-of-the-rudeboy-exhibition-somerset-house-video">
          <img alt="channel4 news" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/ac9c1de8-043a-11e4-958d-0a6b09a68d06"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         During last week
         <a href="http://www.channel4.com/news/return-of-the-rudeboy-exhibition-somerset-house-video">
          Channel 4 News
         </a>
         presented a special news feature on the exhibition,
         <a href="https://twitter.com/BOYADEE">
          Boya Dee
         </a>
         came to '
         <a href="http://www.somersethouse.org.uk/visual-arts/return-of-the-rudeboy">
          Return of the Rudeboy
         </a>
         ' and talked to Dean and Harris about the show and the way it has captured the essence of what is happening NOW!... This great feature has some classic old footage and sets the scene very well for those less familiar with the history of Rudeboy culture.
        </p>
        <p>
         Thousands upon thousands have now visited the exhibition and it continues to excite and draw people from right across the spectrum from young to old. People are seeing the show as an important cultural barometer as well as appreciating the sartorial elegance and manner of the subjects in the pictures. The three dimensional objects and the extra
         <a href="http://www.somersethouse.org.uk/visual-arts/return-of-the-rudeboy">
          events
         </a>
         are adding even more experiential depth and the functioning Barbershop on a Thursday and Saturday is certainly proving popular too..So get along to the show if you can,it is onfor a few more weeks but don't miss it..
        </p>
        <p>
         Return of the Rudeboy is open to the publicuntil25th August 2014.
        </p>
        <p>
         Free entry open 10am-6pm everyday (Last entry 5:30pm)
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2014/july/channel_4_news_gets_rude#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2014/july/channel_4_news_gets_rude">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/june/gq_interview_with_dean_and_harris">
         GQ interview with Dean and Harris
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        30 June 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  7:16
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.gq-magazine.co.uk/style/articles/2014-06/23/return-of-the-rudeboys-somerset-house-exhibition">
          <img alt="GQ INTERVIEW" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/26f3ce22-0082-11e4-94d2-0a6b09a68d06"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Click on the link above to read the GQ interview with Dean and Harris it's a good one.
        </p>
        <p>
         There is however a slight inaccuracy, there is a misquote attributed to Dean, itsays, "with a style that goes back to the late Eighties/ early Nineties, when men wore their Nike Air Max sneakers with pin tuck trousers." Dean would like to make it known that he is fully aware that the Rudeboy first emerged in the late 1950's early 1960's and it was only in a much later incarnation that said clothing was involved. We hope that clears the matter up. Tajinder has written a good article so pleaseclick on the picture toread on.
        </p>
       </div>

        <a href="2014/june/gq_interview_with_dean_and_harris#comments">

        <a href="2014/may/the_arena_screened_at_the_southend_film_festival">
         The Arena screened at The Southend Film Festival
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        05 May 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:03
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="the arena film still" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/7200a4dc-d425-11e3-9c16-8293f4fa3655"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Arena will be screened at the
         <a href="http://www.southendfilmfestival.com/">
          Southend Film Festival
         </a>
         Closing Gala this evening. This film festival is a highly rated annual event attracting crowds to watch cutting edge films from around the world over a 5 day period.The final programme for the event this year includes 'The Arena' and the George Harrison psychedelic classic 1968 film 'The Magic Christian'. This will be a great way to conclude what has been a very successful and eventful festival.
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">

         Chrissie Hynde: Album Teaser
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        11 April 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:22
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/chrissiehynde/photos/a.375847289112264.91780.269715306392130/735741116456211/?type=1&amp;theater">
          <img alt="Chrissie Hynde Album " src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/794d6c54-c1ae-11e3-89d1-76121a5c6bd2"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Chrissie Hynde is one of the most iconic women in rock music, an amazing character that stands up for her beliefs, her influence and creativity has not only stood the test of time but continues to flourish producing more and more great pieces of music. It may suprise many thatStockholmis the first solo album, This new collection iseagerly anticipated.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean shot theStockholmalbum cover and art work as well as manyother images of Chrissie that will emerge as the release of the album approaches. Click on the picture above and link to the competition that's prize is a very special night where Chrissie will perform tracks from Stockholm.

         Holly Willoughby for the Observer Magazine
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        30 March 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 11:19
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt=""/>

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/march/return_of_the_rudeboy_exhibition_at_somerset_house">
         Return of the Rudeboy : Exhibition at Somerset House
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        09 March 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:50
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <strong>
          <img alt="Untitled" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/d46ae5ce-a6f3-11e3-bb9a-9604fab9f27a"/>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Return of the Rudeboy
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Dean Chalkley x Harris Elliott
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          13 June  25 August 201
         </strong>
         4
         <br/>
         <strong>
          Daily 10.00-18.00
         </strong>
         <br/>
         <strong>
          Terrace Rooms, South Wing
         </strong>
         <br/>
         <strong>
          Free admission
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         This summeris certainly going to be a lively time on the embankment, Dean has linked up withcreative director Harris Elliott to present"Return of the Rudeboy" at
         <a href="http://www.somersethouse.org.uk/visual-arts/return-of-the-rudeboy">
          Somerset House
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         This original exhibition will reflect asartorial subculture through a series of portraits, installations and set pieces.
        </p>
        <p>
         For the last yearDean and Harris have been working on this great new project,shootingover 60 sharply dressed individuals from across the UK, all embody the essence of what it is to be a Rudeboy (or Rudie) in the 21st century. The curated collection of images show subjects presenting their pure and singular sartorial swagger in locations linked to the Rudeboy lifestyle, whether it be on the streets of Shoreditch or Savile Row.
        </p>
        <p>
         The exhibition will be an immersive experience of visuals and sounds, taking visitors into the worlds of todays Rudeboys. Each of the subjects featured in the portraits have provided their signature playlist, which will be amalgamated along with curators and collaborators choices into a soundtrack to capture the spirit and soul of the Rudeboy, acting as a sonic backdrop to the visual works. Since grooming is integral to the Rudeboy routine, the space will host a pop-up grooming station where visitors can book appointments to get their hair cut or beard trimmed by a top Rudeboy barber. Working with artisan box maker Kitty Farrow and luggage manufacturer Alstermo, bespoke brief cases, hat boxes and luggage sets will be made to show how this collective of individuals pays attention to detail in all aspects with their fashions.
        </p>
        <p>
         In true Rudeboy style, Chalkley and Elliott have collaborated closely with a variety of inspirational and influential creative minds to contribute exciting, engaging and enriching content to the exhibition. These include Rashad Smith, a British-born, New York-based producer who has worked with the likes of The Notorious B.I.G, Busta Rhymes and Nas; the Art Comes First creative collective founded by top travelling tailors Sam Lambert and Shaka Maidoh; and founding member of Big Audio Dynamite, Grammy award-winning filmmaker and international DJ Don Letts, a pillar of the punk and reggae scene who inspired a generation through his groundbreaking music, films and fashions.
        </p>
        <p>
         There will also be an exciting season of events in conjunction with the exhibition for visitors to exchange and enrich their knowledge and understanding of this important and culturally significant subculture, from film screenings to sartorial workshops. The events will pay respect to the heritage and importance of the past, but focus on the present and future Rudeboy.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         So look our for
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Website
         <a href="http://www.ReturnoftheRudeboy.com">
          www.ReturnoftheRudeboy.com
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Twitter @RudeboysReturn
        </p>
        <p>
         Intsagram @RudeboysReturn
        </p>
        <p>
         Face Book
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/returnoftherudeboy">
          https://www.facebook.com/returnoftherudeboy
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         We are all very excited about this season of events that will span a two month period,so watch this and those spaces for hot news.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2014/march/return_of_the_rudeboy_exhibition_at_somerset_house#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2014/march/return_of_the_rudeboy_exhibition_at_somerset_house">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/january/daft_punk_grammy_winners">
         Daft Punk : Grammy Winners
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        27 January 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:12
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="Daft Punk grammy winners" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/e6a7fb48-878e-11e3-8b9e-4ae51eaeb824"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         deanchalkley/nme/ipcmedia
        </p>
        <p>
         Congratulations to Daft Punk for their well deserved
         <a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/entertainment-arts-25850644">
          Grammy wins
         </a>
         last night. The robotic masters bagged five awards on the night including the two biggest prizes 'Record' and 'Album' of the Year. Dean shot Daft Punk for NME during 2013, the images were released to coincide with the launch of the electronic duos amazing album 'Random Access Memories' you can get it
         <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/gb/artist/daft-punk/id5468295">
          here
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         Daft Punk are seldom (like virtually never) seen without their helmets, ...we bet you wish you could see the frame after the one below hey... But we wouldn't want to show you all the roboty insides that lay beneath their shiny exterior, so the mystique must remain... They are truly out of this world though aren't they?
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Daft Punk grammy winners" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/2dd84658-878f-11e3-a701-4ae51eaeb824"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         deanchalkley/nme/ipcmedia
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2014/january/daft_punk_grammy_winners#comments">

        <a href="2014/january/steve_mcqueen_exhibition">
         Steve McQueen Exhibition
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        10 January 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:27
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="Steve McQueen Exhibition" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/95e9f322-7a3d-11e3-a141-4ae51eaeb824"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Steve McQueen was of course a massive film star, but he was a style Icon too. We thought it was only right to tell you about an exhibition that has been created in his honour "I live for myself and I answer to nobody" Comprises of photography from the legendary Barry Feinstein (you can see one through the cars window above), The Mustang car (above) from the film Bullet, Motor bikes clothing etc, also there is a section of items that have been influenced by Steve McQueen.
        </p>
        <p>
         It is all very good and free to enter.
         <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.co.uk/2013/11/22/steve-mcqueen-unseen-pictures-bullitt-barry-feinstein_n_4324667.html">
          Here
         </a>
         is a great interview from the Huffington Post, and for even more info on the show click
         <a href="http://www.influx.co.uk/wordpress/blog/steve-mcqueen-exhibition/#sthash.4NXThe20.dpbs">
          here
         </a>
         ...One word of advice though, when visiting the exhibition take a big coat it is on the 3rd floor of Brewer Street Car Park and it is cold.
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2014/january/london_collections_mens_">
         London Collections: Mens
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        10 January 14
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:43
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="agi &amp; Sam fashion Show 1" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/be451b72-7a37-11e3-81a0-4ae51eaeb824"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         deanchalkley
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.londoncollections.co.uk">
          London Collections: Mens
         </a>
         was a great success packed days of shows, meetings and exciting new outfits to see about town. The centre of London was peppered with striking people dashing from place to place, day and night the catwalks boomed and the parties rolled.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean went to the packed early morning
         <a href="http://agiandsam.tumblr.com/">
          Agi &amp; Sam
         </a>
         show in Bloomsbury on Wednesday. It took place on the last day of the events.
         <a href="http://www.londoncollections.co.uk/schedule_aw14.aspx">
          Here
         </a>
         is a list of all the shows.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://harriselliott.com/">
          Harris Elliott
         </a>
         acted as creative director to this show (also the Mr.Hare presentation in our previous post) Gary Powell was commisioned to provide the soundtrack for the show. Gary conducted 4 live drummers that morning, the ex-Libertines drummer is a very experienced composer and has provided many scores for films and fashion shows.
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/december/merry_christmas_">
         Merry Christmas !!
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        26 December 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:58
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>

         </em>

         Come Down to the Bang &amp; Olufsen Store in Swiss Cottage on Saturday the 14th Dec. Dean's making a short film and taking a few shots of DB Cohen playing an Instore accompanied by the B&amp;O wonder box the Beolit 12. From 10:30am the first 10 people who come in the store for the gig will be given a free DB Cohen CD. After 11 am DB Cohen will Perform a number of Songs. This session will be filmed and photographed. After the Instore session the filming will continue in Swiss Cottage and in Camden Town.         </p>
        <p>
         125 Magazine have produced a fantastic new book. Entitled 'X' it marks the tenth anniversary of the publications existence and contains many of its best features from the past decade. Copies of the book can be picked up at selected bookshops and galleries and the Magazine have a special pop up book shop at 123 Bethnal Green Road London E2 7DG (open till Sunday 9th Dec). This first edition numbered run is limited to only 1250 copies so snap one up before they go. Click

        <a href="2013/november/adidas_originals_blue_fw13">
         Adidas Originals Blue FW13
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        22 November 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  6:38
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="adidas" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/f726ee02-53a4-11e3-9e57-1e749ce2aaf3"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Recently Dean collaborated with creative director
         <a href="http://www.harriselliott.com/">
          Harris
         </a>
         Elliotton the FW13
         <a href="http://www.adidas.co.uk/originals_blue">
          Adidas Originals Blue Campaign
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         This collection has heritage and lux Street styles combing the two sartorial approaches seamlessly. As the Adidas statement says there is an undercurrent of sub-culture in these styles they also have a great feeling of cosmopolitan flare.
        </p>
        <p>
         The shoot took place in Shoreditch Studios with sets that reflected the essence of the collections direction. Certainly inner-city life brought to life.
        </p>
        <p>
         There will be more of this series posted soon in the fashion section of the site, so keep an eye out for that.
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/november/chas_and_dave_thats_what_happens_album_cover">
         Chas &amp; Dave: 'That's What Happens' Album Cover
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        15 November 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:59
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="Chas and Dave" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/7f9529e2-4e38-11e3-8d6b-f614dfb8f2c3"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         'That's What Happens' is the new album by legends Chas &amp; Dave. Dean stepped out with the fellas to shoot the album cover and press images. The album has received critical acclaim and finds the chaps in top form this is what the Guardian say about the album:Chas Hodges and Dave Peacock's first studio album in 18 years will come as a surprise to those who remember their hit-making heyday. They've been working together for 50 years now and this collection of covers harks back to their skiffle and blues roots. There are echoes of Leadbelly and country harmonies on the likes of opener Railroad Billand Midnight Special, and Hodges's voice has a kind of grit to it that only age and experience can provide on numbers such as Right String Baby. The old joanna doesn't even show up till the swinging, full-band single When Two Worlds Collide, and the only "rockney" track proper is piano-and-bass workout Rocking Gloworm. New Orleans march All By Myself closes the album with solos by Jools Holland and Hugh Laurie, but it's the jazzy I Can't Give You Anything But Love and the penultimate track Glory of Love, both featuring Martin Taylor on guitar, that are the real gems... Click
         <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=H-PRklG4W7E">
          HERE
         </a>
         to see them performing Railroad Bill on Mr. Holland's show
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2013/november/chas_and_dave_thats_what_happens_album_cover#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2013/november/chas_and_dave_thats_what_happens_album_cover">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/october/a_night_for_jon_brookes">
         A Night for Jon Brookes
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        18 October 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:20
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="A Tribute to Jon Brookes Poster" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/55e7c064-37d6-11e3-aa0e-8a5f241601c0"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Tonight at the Royal Albert Hall there is a special charity event 'A Night for Jon Brookes'. The Charlatans released an official statement that read "Following the loss of our much missed friend and drummer, Jon Brookes, we, together with some friends, are putting on a show at the Royal Albert Hall. The show will benefit The Brain Tumour Charity, which Jon was involved with during his illness. Its our way of raising money for research into and awareness of a cancer that will unfortunately affect many lives as it has ours. We look forward to seeing you at the Royal Albert Hall and making it a night to remember." To find out more details please go to The Charlatans Official website
         <a href="http://www.thecharlatans.net/news.php">
          HERE
         </a>
         .Dean has been documenting the rehearsals and preparations for the event and will also be taking photographs tonight. Artist
         <a href="http://www.monsterism.net/">
          Pete Fowler
         </a>
         has created the poster above for A Night for Jon Brookes at the Royal Albert Hall show. Limited edition prints will be available on the night.
        </p>
       </div>

         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2013/october/a_night_for_jon_brookes">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>

        <a href="2013/september/the_new_british_at_the_vanda">
         The New British at the V&amp;A
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        29 September 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:10
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="The New British at the V&amp;A" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/01a6caa2-222a-11e3-a0e4-7606b0b1d62a"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="The New British at the V&amp;A snaps" height="327" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/7ef11c38-28f6-11e3-a986-8a5f241601c0" width="245"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         dean chalkley
        </p>
        <p>
         'The Arena' is Deans latest film: Screened at the V&amp;A Museum London on Friday 27th September 2013 as part of it's Friday Lates sessions. The film spins around the Crash Bang Wallop World of Banger Racing, a 12 minute long ode to the sport and various characters from the Spedeworth Racing Track in Aldershot.
        </p>
        <p>
         The New British Magazine was invited into the V&amp;A to curate a space and present works that reflected the theme of Destruction. Kez Glozier the Magazines editor brought together works for several different artists to present an emotional informative and at times hard hitting selection of moving image pieces that reflect the essence of The New British's reason for being.
        </p>
        <p>
         'The Arena' film is not the end of the project, like all the works they point to more facets that will be announced soon, so watch this space, the
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/groups/132952516774309/">
          Facebook page
         </a>
         and
         <a href="https://twitter.com/Chalkley_News">
          @Chalkley_News
         </a>
         on Twitter for details.
        </p>
        <p>
         <em>
          original post:
          <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thenew.british.9?hc_location=timeline">
           The V&amp;A : 27th September : The New British
          </a>
          : Dean will unveil elements of his latest project, he will screen a short filmon Banger Racing in Britain. 6:30pm-10pm free entry places are designated on a first come, first served basis, this is an event not to be missed, For more details click
          <a href="http://www.vam.ac.uk/content/articles/f/friday-late/">
           here
          </a>
          .
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/september/tim_peaks_diner_action">
         Tim Peaks Diner Action
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        10 September 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  3:56
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="tim peaks" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/ea7cf33c-1a2d-11e3-92b6-7606b0b1d62a"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Craige Barker
        </p>
        <p>
         Today
         <a href="http://www.timpeaks.com/">
          Tim Peaks Diner
         </a>
         has a special day. It celebrates the opening of its first pop-up Diner in the HMV store in Cambridge. Tim Burgess asked Dean if he'd like to pop-up a few pictures on the wall, and of course Dean said yes, the whole Tim Peaks thing is an ongoing organic creative development.
        </p>
        <p>
         Oh and what a place the HMV in Cambridge is too ! A grade 2 listed building with 3 floors of music games and books ..and now a Tim Peaks Diner amongst it...how good is that...
        </p>
        <p>
         The photograph of Dean was shot by
         <a href="http://www.craigebarker.com">
          Craige Barker
         </a>
         , taken on 9th Sept when Dean visited the store to see it all coming together. The photograph of Tim was originally shot for the
         <a href="http://www.nme.com/">
          NME magazine
         </a>
         and can be seen in the gallery on this site click
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/gallery/music/">
          here
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         This coming weekend the Diner pops up once again , this time inPortmeirion at the brilliant
         <a href="http://www.festivalnumber6.com/">
          Festival No6
         </a>
         Dean and the Black Cat Djs this time including Sonny
         <a href="http://theuglysoundsystem.tumblr.com/">
          Scully
         </a>
         Evans and
         <a href="http://www.hemingwaydesign.co.uk/teams/16">
          Jack Hemingway
         </a>
         (this link is more about him in general, anyhow) they will also be spinning the vinyl , getting the people dancing and making the place jump to the
         <a href="http://radio.novalujon.com/03-04-13-dean-chalkley/">
          Rhythm and Soul sounds
         </a>
         Black Cat is known for....
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/august/society_maybe_you_heard_it_here_first">
         SOCIETY: Maybe you heard it here first...
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        29 August 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:37
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="society" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/f736d1ea-10de-11e3-b82c-720952d2a5e4"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Society
         </strong>
         have released their highly anticipated second single
         <strong>
          '14 Hours' (Click
         </strong>
         <strong>
          <a href="http://www.thefader.com/2013/08/01/stream-society-14-hours/">
           here
          </a>
          )
         </strong>
         . Shooting to infamy late last year on the back of the runaway success of a super-limited 7-inch vinyl-only debut called 'All That We've Become',they achieved major plaudits Radio
         <strong>
          1
         </strong>
         and
         <strong>
          6Music
         </strong>
         <strong>
         </strong>
         loved them as did them NMEand
         <strong>
          Q
         </strong>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         '14 Hours' is a special release via the
         <strong>
          Angular Recording Corporation
         </strong>
         the people who brought you These New Puritans, Klaxons, Bloc Party etc so you know this is going to be quality and weighty. The man behind this hunting and chilling croon is, 24-year-old London-based,
         <strong>
          James Girdler
         </strong>
         , Dean photographed James for the bands first and very cinematic press session this is a malevolent image isn't it...
        </p>
        <p>
         You will be hearing much more from Society soon..but for now, listen to their deep haunting
         <a href="http://thequietus.com/articles/12972-society-14-hours">
          14 Hours
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
