       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/august/hush_puppies_the_darkroom">
         Hush Puppies: The  Darkroom
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        16 August 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  3:21
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="gal" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/99d2a570-10e7-11e3-b024-7606b0b1d62a"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/events/225554334262019/">
          THE HUSH PUPPIES POP UP DARKROOM
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         From Friday 23rd August  Monday 26th August, Hush Puppies will be opening the doors of Truman Brewery and welcoming the creative and curious in for an exploration into traditional photography as part of their new pop-up Darkroom.
        </p>
        <p>
         Taking budding photographers back in time to the days of old school processes and analogue cameras, the vast space just off Brick Lane, in the East of London will reveal all.
        </p>
        <p>
         Guests can rent a 35mm film camera, hit the streets of London with their analogue in tow and on return personally print their own favourite image in the Darkroom with experts on hand to help guide people through the process.
        </p>
        <p>
         Throughout the four days of the pop up there will be a line-up of dynamic experts hosting interactive workshops too, these include learning how to make your own retro-pinhole camera, taking a tour with street photography experts who will help you take the perfectpictureand then take you back to the Darkroom to develop your masterpiece. As well as a pop-up classic camera store from photography specialists Films Not Dead.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean Chalkley will be exhibiting a sample of images from'The Executioners' (see image above), a new and previously unseen photographic essay that portrays members of an obscurerenegade British Car Club.Dean comented: If you are using film on a shoot there's always an element of surprise, anticipation and excitement. Nowadays so many images are viewed On-screen, which is all good, but the beauty and physicality of a real photographic print and conventional photographic process is still a very special thing  Id definitely encourage everyone to experience it.Im delighted to be displaying this series of images at the Darkroom. I had to think differently on this shoot, relinquish a bit of control, but this slightly different approach has reignited my appreciation of doing things this way. I hope it will produce similar feelings in those getting involved and taking part in the Darkroom.
        </p>
        <p>
         Photographer and award-winning fine art printer Debbie Sears will be running the Darkroom for more info on all of this check out
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/HushPuppiesUK">
          Hush Puppies
         </a>
         site.
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/HushPuppiesUK">
          <br/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2013/august/hush_puppies_the_darkroom#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2013/august/hush_puppies_the_darkroom">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/august/modernists_gather_in_brighton_for_august_bank_holiday_">
         Modernists gather in Brighton for August Bank Holiday
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        15 August 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  6:14
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="scooter" height="542" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/30e1f90e-10e6-11e3-8a1a-7606b0b1d62a" width="542"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         If you want to hang out with the cream of the Mod scene, see some great scooters and dance to the very best in Modernist sounds then get down to Brighton on the August Bank Holiday. In case you are unfamiliar with Brightons significance to the Mod scene, check out
         <a href="http://www.modculture.co.uk/">
          Mod Culture
         </a>
         website and you can find out lots of good information. It is the annual New Untouchables weekender. The holiday weekend will be jam packed with wonder, there is so much going on down there you must check out The New Untouchables site. Dean will be Djing at the Volts on the Sunday night for the second year on the trot. For full details of the weekend click
         <a href="http://www.newuntouchables.com/home/?portfolio=brighton-weekender">
          here
         </a>
         . Click
         <a href="http://www.ticketweb.co.uk/event/60691">
          here
         </a>
         for tickets for the Saturday night. For the Sunday night event at the Volts featuring NUT's Dj's and special guest DJ slots but Pete and &amp; Chris Tebbutt and Dean click
         <a href="http://www.ticketweb.co.uk/event/62725">
          here
         </a>
         or just pop down and enjoy the sun.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean will be warming up for the Brighton Weekender at
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/events/567099633331969/">
          Black Cat
         </a>
         this Saturday so pop along to the The Silver Bullet in Finsbury Park this Saturday if you can.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/august/tim_peaks_oh_no_i_love_you">
         Tim Peaks ..Oh No I Love You..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        04 August 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:30
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p style="margin-top: .1pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: .1pt; margin-left: 0cm;">
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top: .1pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: .1pt; margin-left: 0cm;">
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top: .1pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: .1pt; margin-left: 0cm;">
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top: .1pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: .1pt; margin-left: 0cm;">
         <img alt="Tim Peaks Diner at Kendal Calling 2" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/cf6c11ba-fba4-11e2-8f2d-6e16d116e55f"/>
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top: .1pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: .1pt; margin-left: 0cm;">
         deanchalkley/camerapress
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top: .1pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: .1pt; margin-left: 0cm;">
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top: .1pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: .1pt; margin-left: 0cm;">
         <span style="font-size: 9.0pt; font-family: Verdana; color: black;">
          <a href="http://www.timpeaks.com/">
           Tim Peaks
          </a>
          Diner was brilliant! This small log cabin was the perfect setting for intimate performances, discussions and interviews. Great live music and Deejays (inc
          <a href="https://twitter.com/BlackCatDJs">
           Black Cat Djs
          </a>
          and
          <a href="http://www.davehaslam.com/">
           Dave Haslam
          </a>
          as well as creative Master classes presented by Record Producers, eminent Journalists, Cartoonists etc, Dean delivered one too on photography (
          <a href="http://www.cumbrialive.co.uk/home/kendal-calling-review-dean-chalkley-masterclass-1.1073635">
           review
          </a>
          ). The weekends schedule was packed with so much good stuff! Spontaneous acoustic performances by
          <a href="http://johnainsworthmusic.com/">
           John Ainsworth
          </a>
          and
          <a href="http://www.thetwistedwheel.co.uk/preorder/">
           Twisted Wheel
          </a>
          , M
          <a href="http://www.musicalbingo.co.uk/">
           usical Bingo
          </a>
          even so you can see the scope of what was happening in this Hansel and Gretel like cabin...Well, the cake and Tim Peaks Coffee flowed and there were smiles all round, Tim Burgess played in the Diner on Sunday afternoon and it was amazing (picture above) People squeezed in 'til the cabin was full, people even watched through the windows trying to soak up the very special atmosphere. Legendary! (check out the '
          <a href="http://louderthanwar.com/tim-peaks-diner-kendal-calling-2013-festival-review/">
           Louder than War
          </a>
          ' blog about it)
         </span>
        </p>
        <p style="margin-top: .1pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: .1pt; margin-left: 0cm;">
         <span style="font-size: 9.0pt; font-family: Verdana; color: black;">
          The Diner was of course part of the
          <a href="http://www.kendalcalling.co.uk/">
           Kendal Calling festival
          </a>
          set in the Lake District amongst beautiful countryside and very well organised there was always enough great music, food and.er...loos... Even a bit of a down pour on the Saturday night didn't interrupt the universal fun for everyone.... Like Kendal Mint Cake ..It Was Sweet!!...er her..did you like that??..
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>

         </fb:comments-count>

        </a>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/july/adidas_originals_blue_collection_fw13">
         Adidas Originals Blue Collection FW13
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        24 July 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  2:47
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/fd8d301e-f0a6-11e2-a5db-fa3410ec1e25"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Due for release shortly is Adidas' Originals Blue Collection FW13 with a campaign shot by Dean Chalkley.
        </p>
        <p>
         The Adidas Originals Blue collection is a premium apparel and footwear line intertwining adidass impeccable lifestyle heritage with a luxury street aesthetic. Mixing functional sport utilitarianism with street attitude, the FW13 collection perfectly combines the two sartorial disciplines by focusing on versatile trainers and clothes. A sub-cultural edge is thrown into the mix, giving adidas Originals Blue an attitude worthy of any street corner in London, Berlin, Paris, Tokyo or New York.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/0b18ee08-f0a7-11e2-8c41-6e16d116e55f"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/a882c1a2-f465-11e2-aa1c-6e16d116e55f"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Prints clash but the colours match; adidas Originals Blue fuse all-over graphics, rock iconology, hip-hop culture, subversive camouflage and patterns from the animal kingdom. Innovative details, such as taped seams and technical zips, and high-tech water-repellent materials keep you on track. Classic basketball uniforms share the court with running gear re-appropriated for inner-city life.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/b3b5f346-f465-11e2-a6a3-fa3410ec1e25"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>

        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        19 July 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:59
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/1bfd9f18-f451-11e2-b702-6e16d116e55f"/>
        </p>
        <h6>
          Dean Chalkley 2013
        </h6>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p class="p1">
         Dean has is now back in the UK following his trip to attend the eagerly anticipated private view of his new group exhibition You Ain't Seen Nothing Yet in Antwerp.
        </p>
        <p class="p2">
        </p>
        <p class="p1">
         The opening night was 1100 strong parting in to the early hours, helped along the way with a DJ set from homegrown talent Tom Barman from Deus.
        </p>
        <p class="p2">
        </p>
        <p class="p2">
         <img alt="" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/3c6f4ebc-f452-11e2-9fa2-6e16d116e55f"/>
        </p>
        <h6 class="p2">
          Dean Chalkley 2013
        </h6>
        <p class="p2">
        </p>
        <p class="p2">
         <img alt="" src="http://media.digitalphotogallery.com/fxyrcnkrfzfa/images/d507e696-f454-11e2-908e-fa3410ec1e25/yasny301_blog_image.jpg"/>
        </p>
        <h6 class="p2">
          Guy Voet 2013
        </h6>
        <p class="p2">
        </p>
        <p class="p1">
         The exhibition, which focuses on modern day music photography continues to be shown throughout the summer until 06.10.13.
        </p>
        <p class="p2">
        </p>
        <p class="p1">
         Click
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?v=621209644563934%20">

         to view a short video that previewed the show, test your Dutch and see if you can spot anyone familiar :)

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/june/you_aint_seen_nothing_yet">
         You Ain't Seen Nothing Yet.
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        13 June 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  2:52
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="You aint seen nothing yet" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/431a47a6-d366-11e2-bcad-028bb35adaf5"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Music and photography are inseparably linked.
         <a href="http://www.fotomuseum.be/" target="_blank">
          <strong>
           <em>
            You Ain't Seen Nothing Yet
           </em>
          </strong>
         </a>
         shows the work of photographers who stand out for their unique style and original approach. The exhibition in Antwerp Belgiumincludes intimate backstage portraits, eccentric group portraits and iconic album covers. FoMu is showing work by, among others,
         <strong>
          Dean Chalkley
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          Joris Bulckens
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          Daniel Cohen
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          Charlie De Keersmaeker
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          Koen Keppen
         </strong>
         s,
         <strong>
          Ryan McGinley
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          James Mollison
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          Alex Salians
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          Michael Schmelling
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          Oliver Sieber
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          Alex Vanhee
         </strong>
         ,
         <strong>
          Eva Vermandel
         </strong>
         and
         <strong>
          Rob Walbers
         </strong>
         . The exhibition includes album cover art, music videos, photography books and an installation by Radio Soulwax.
        </p>
        <p>
         You Aint Seen Nothing Yet Exhibtionat FoMu runs from28.06.13 - 06.10.13
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/june/water_aid_pump_up_the_volume">
         Water Aid Pump Up The Volume
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        12 June 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  6:12
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="" height="401" src="http://www.wateraid.org/uk/~/media/Images/UK/Photo%20gallery%20-%20645x401/Glastonbury%202013/Tim-Burgess-2.ashx" width="645"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         We are extremely proud to announce Deans involvement in Water Aids latest amazing awareness campaign Pump up the Volume.
        </p>
        <p>
         The Campaign asks Glastonbury 2013 festival-goers to
         <a href="http://e-activist.com/ea-action/action?ea.client.id=1676&amp;ea.campaign.id=20102&amp;ea.tracking.id=banner&amp;__utma=1.1971807103.1372072153.1372073676.1372073676.3&amp;__utmb=1.1.10.1372073676&amp;__utmc=1&amp;__utmx=-&amp;__utmz=1.1372073676.2.2.utmcsr=google|utmccn=(organic)|utmcmd=organic|utmctr=(not%20provided)&amp;__utmv=-&amp;__utmk=135828145">
          Pump up the Volume
         </a>
          for a world were everyone, everywhere has safe water and sanitation by 2030. Water Aid will be all over the site gathering signatures that will then be taken to the UN in September, calling for universal access to safe water and sanitation. At their stand, you will be able to support the campaign by having your photo as you Pump up the volume. But you dont have to be at Glastonbury this year to take part and show your support. Click here to sign their
         <a href="http://e-activist.com/ea-action/action?ea.client.id=1676&amp;ea.campaign.id=20102&amp;ea.tracking.id=banner&amp;__utma=1.1971807103.1372072153.1372073676.1372073676.3&amp;__utmb=1.1.10.1372073676&amp;__utmc=1&amp;__utmx=-&amp;__utmz=1.1372073676.2.2.utmcsr=google|utmccn=(organic)|utmcmd=organic|utmctr=(not%20provided)&amp;__utmv=-&amp;__utmk=135828145">
          Epetition
         </a>
         .
        </p>

       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        11 June 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:31
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Liam NME cover" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/1244610a-cf8a-11e2-8aa6-42b27fde8898"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean has shot Liam Gallagher many times now, In fact Deans first ever encounter with Liam, Noel and the rest of Oasis was at the
         <a href="http://chelmsfordrocks.com/armyandnavy.html">
          Army and Navy pub in Chelmsford
         </a>
         way back in the 1990's. Dean was in a very embryonic stage of his photography, always connected to the music scene and went to the 'Army and Navy' to check out this band that had a great buzz about them. The gig was by all accounts incredible, Dean positioned himself to the right of the small stage and awaited the band, when Liam walked onto the stage he spotted the Camera and thrust 2 fingers virtually into the lens...Whooohhh ...what an Attitude...Apparently the gigwas amazing and the crowd went crazy, people dancing on the pubs counter as theband thrilled the eager the very excitable hipsters squeezed into this small venue.. Oasis finished their set with a cover of the Beatles classic 'I Am The Walrus'.
        </p>
        <p>
         That was a long time ago though, and much has changed... Oasis went through several different line-ups and became massive of course. The legendary relationship between the Gallagher brothers has exploded across the media on more than one occasion.
        </p>
        <p>
         Both Noel and Liam now have very successful solo careers,Liam's splinter outfit is called 'Beady Eye' and they have just released their 3rd album since splitting up Oasis. The new collection of tracks it called "BE' and can be heard on Spotify, check out Beady Eye's website
         <a href="http://www.beadyeyemusic.com/">
          here
         </a>
         for more information about the band gigs and all that jazz....
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2013/june/beady_eye_nme#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2013/june/beady_eye_nme">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/june/125_magazine_is_out">
         125 Magazine is out!!
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        11 June 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:20
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="valerie june 125 magazine" height="419" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/a362ade4-d26f-11e2-a223-42b27fde8898" width="419"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         The New Edition of 125 Magazine is out, 219 pages of juicy stuff including great editorial photographic features 'Wayne's World' by Rick Guest, God's Fondness by Tim Flach and Valerie June by Dean. This thick heavy bound magazine is available from good News Agents, Art Book stores, Galleries and online
         <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/">
          here
         </a>
         .
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/may/daft_punk_top_secret_mission_to_paris">
         Daft Punk Top Secret Mission To Paris
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        20 May 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  4:04
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="daft punk cover" height="496" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/fe985800-c15b-11e2-b28b-42b27fde8898" width="402"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Eight years after their last album, the dynamic French duo
         <a href="http://www.daftpunk.com/" target="_blank" title="Daft Punk">
          Daft Punk
         </a>
         have released an explosive new album!
        </p>
        <p>
         This fourth studio album entitled
         <a href="http://www.randomaccessmemories.com/" target="_blank">
          <em>
           Random Access Memories
          </em>
         </a>
         is available today in the UK.
        </p>
        <p>
         It is a phenomenal piece of work!
        </p>
        <p>
         Recorded over five years in studios in Paris, London, and New York and reputed to have cost several million dollars to make
         <em>
          Random Access Memories
         </em>
         features collaborations with legends such as
         <a href="http://www.moroder.net/" target="_blank">
          Giorgio Moroder
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.nilerodgers.com/" target="_blank">
          Nile Rodgers
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Panda_Bear_(musician)" target="_blank">
          Panda Bear
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.juliancasablancas.com/" target="_blank">
          Julian Casablancas
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Todd_Edwards" target="_blank">
          Todd Edwards
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.myspace.com/djfalconparis" target="_blank">
          DjFalcon
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://chillygonzales.com/" target="_blank">
          ChillyGonzales
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paul_Williams_(songwriter)" target="_blank">
          Paul Williams
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://pharrellwilliams.com/" target="_blank">
          Pharrell Williams
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         Back to the shoot
        </p>
        <p>
         Although shrouded in mystery we can say that Dean travelled on a very secret mission to Paris and encountered the two maestros.
        </p>
        <p>
         Daft Punk were interviewed in
         <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2010/11/02/former-bing-crosby-estate_n_777161.html#s171024" target="_blank">
          Bing Crosby's former mansion
         </a>
         in California for the NME Magazine.
        </p>
        <p>
         The piece appears in the current issue and, you can take a look on
         <a href="http://www.nme.com/magazine/issue/daft-punk-exclusive" target="_blank">
          NME.com
         </a>
         to see a taster of the article and other Daft Punk stuff!!! Click here to go to
         <a href="https://play.spotify.com/?utm_source=spotify.com&amp;utm_medium=redirect&amp;utm_campaign=spotify_autoredirect" target="_blank">
          spotify
         </a>
         to hear the album.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2013/may/daft_punk_top_secret_mission_to_paris#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2013/may/daft_punk_top_secret_mission_to_paris">
         </fb:comments-count>

        </a>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/may/royal_photographic_magazine_feature_">
         Royal Photographic Magazine Feature
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        04 May 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 11:06
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="RPS Magazine" height="403" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/1f75062a-b4a2-11e2-9327-42b27fde8898" width="403"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         This Months RPS Magazine has just been published. This month there is a 7 page article written by David Land about Dean. The piece focuses on Deans holistic approach, including commentary on his films, installation, and of course photography. The piece is illustrated with a range of images from The New Faces series, Benedict Cumberbatch, Scarlett Johansson and the Cath Kidston and Hush Puppies Campaigns as well as other photographs shot by Dean. The RPS Magazine is subscription only but the RPS can be contacted through their www.facebook.com/royalphotographicsocietyor friend them on twitter @The_RPS
        </p>

       </h3>

       </h3>

         </a>

        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        06 April 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  6:24
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="dean chalkley portrait" height="383" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/5a782386-9ee2-11e2-9f4f-fefd616b8533" width="264"/>

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/april/shortlist_out_today_with_feature_on_mod_a_very_british_style_">
         Shortlist out today with feature on MOD: A Very British Style
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        04 April 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:51
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="shortlist cover 4-4-13 Mod" height="261" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/51617c42-9d26-11e2-bd15-f23c91df768a" width="261"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.shortlist.com/">
          Shortlist Magazine
         </a>
         today features an article on "How MOD changed the world"; it refers to Richard Weight's recently released book that plots the history of the Sub Culture, its influences heritage and enduring impact. Shortlist's feature includes anecdotes about Scooters,
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Stephen">
          John Stephen
         </a>
         , The Sassoon Hair Cuts,
         <a href="http://www.bluenote.com/">
          Blue Note Records
         </a>
         and other sonic, sartorial and things the Mod (Modernist) culture incorporates. Two of
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/thenewfaces/">
          The New Faces
         </a>
         images are included in the piece.
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/march/mod_a_very_british_style_">
         MOD: A Very British Style
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        25 March 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 11:31
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="MOD: A Very British Style" height="565" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/445c04ec-9536-11e2-a5c8-f23c91df768a" width="400"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         This Thursday (28th March at
         <a href="http://www.eastvillageclub.co.uk/">
          East Village Lounge
         </a>
         ,) Richard Weight unveils his new book '
         <a href="http://blogs.spectator.co.uk/books/2013/03/review-mod-a-very-british-style-by-richard-weight/">
          MOD: A Very British Style
         </a>
         '.
        </p>
        <p>
         The publication charts the 'Modernist' Culture from its origins in 1950s Soho to the modern day.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Mod! is a book about the distinctively British youth cult and the artistic and social influence it has had. What became known as Mod was an amalgam of American and European music, fashion and design that has left its mark not only on a variety of subsequent youth cults but also on British culture as a whole. At its peak, in the mid-1960s, Mod became shorthand for what it meant to be a modern Briton; it helped to shape popular ideas about social relationships, taste, lifestyle and national identity at a time when the British Empire was being dismantled and American consumerism was changing British society. - Richard Weight.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         A selection of Dean's
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/thenewfaces/photographic_exhibition/">
          New Faces
         </a>
         Photographs adorn the cover of the book.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         The opening night promises to be a big party!
         <a href="http://www.tonykofimusic.com/">
          Tony Kofi
         </a>
         will DJ as well as a number of special guests selectors!! It's going to be amazing!!
        </p>
        <p>
         For those who don't know Richard Weight, "is a social historian and broadcaster and the author of several books, including
         <em>
          Patriots: National Identity in Britain 19402000
         </em>
         and
         <em>
          The AZ Guide to Modern Britain
         </em>
         . He writes and presents documentaries for the BBC, is a contributor to
         <em>
          The Times,
         </em>
         and is a fellow of the Royal Historical Society and of the Royal Society of Arts. He lectures in Europe and Africa for the British Council and acts as a consultant to several organisations, including the Institute for Public Policy Research."
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         You can find the book at
         <a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Richard-Weight/e/B001HPK7XC">
          amazon
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.bookdepository.co.uk/Mod-Richard-Weight/9780224073912">
          book depository
         </a>
         and at
         <a href="http://www.guardianbookshop.co.uk/BerteShopWeb/viewProduct.do?ISBN=9780224073912">
          guardian bookshop
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2013/march/mod_a_very_british_style_#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2013/march/mod_a_very_british_style_">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/march/david_bowie_is">
         David Bowie: IS
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        21 March 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:13
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/entertainment-arts-21841487">
          David Bowie: IS
         </a>
         Last night the V&amp;A Museum unveiled it's much anticipated David Bowie exhibition.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="David Bowie at the V &amp;A : David Bowie IS" height="581" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/61d340ca-91fe-11e2-877e-f23c91df768a" width="402"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The star-studded private view event was a buzz with movers and shakers. Bowie has of course had a massive effect on the course of popular music for more than 4 decades his creativity and uncompromising approach has penetrated through into general culture. He is a living legend, icon and Transcendental in his appeal he's inspired countless people. This effect is also celebrated in the show, Dean's image of La Roux is included in the show, La Roux is one of the contemporary artists that are clearly highly affected by Bowie. The exhibition has been THE fastest selling shows the V&amp;A has ever put on so if you would like to go to view the seminal show click
         <a href="http://www.vam.ac.uk/content/exhibitions/david-bowie-is/">
          here
         </a>
         to reserve tickets.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Click
         <a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/programmes/b01r11wr">
          here
         </a>
         is a great BBC broadcast ...
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2013/march/david_bowie_is#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2013/march/david_bowie_is">

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/march/did_you_know_dean_djs_">
         Did you know Dean DJ's ?
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        21 March 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:57
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         Here is a little bit of information away from the Photographic and Film side of the activity at Chalkley Towers. For those of you that don't know Dean regularly DJ's and organises club nights around London and other parts of the UK. Soul andRhythm &amp; Blues form the core of his DJ sets but Latin Boogaloo, Rare Groove and other dancefloor filling genres are included in his unique sonic blends. Dean created SHAKE! at the Boogaloo that ran at the imfamous North London Venue The Boogaloo Bar for 4 years (click
         <a href="http://radio.novalujon.com/04-06-11-shake-at-the-boogaloo/">
          here
         </a>
         for a live Radio Nova Lujon broadcast of one of the nights.). After that residency drew to a close Dean and his DJ buddy Si Cheeba started up '
         <a href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/121447371206791/">
          Black Cat
         </a>
         ' at the crutial Club bar The Silver Bullet. Black cat has been running regularly there for 3 years.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean and his fellow Black Cat collective play only Vinyl records....
        </p>
        <p>
         If you want to hear some great records and hit the dancefloor here are a few dates that are coming up that Dean is DJing at:
        </p>
        <p>
         2
         <sup>
          nd
         </sup>
         April
         <a href="http://mamacolive.com/theborderline/listings/upcoming-events/17796/new-street-adventure-plus-new-street-soul-club-djs/">
          New Street Adventure
         </a>
         at The Borderline
        </p>
        <p>
         3rd April Dean will be presenting a
         <a href="http://radio.novalujon.com/category/soup-sessions/">
          Radio Novalujon Soup Session
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         11
         <sup>
          th
         </sup>
         April
         <a href="http://troubadour.co.uk/">
         </a>
         <a href="http://www.londontown.com/LondonInformation/Restaurant/Troubadour/a8ad/events/15237/">
          D.B.Cohen Album Launch Party
         </a>
         at the Troubadour
        </p>
        <p>
         20
         <sup>
          th
         </sup>
         April
         <a href="http://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=10200100075880773&amp;set=a.2758355554176.2144785.1116361669&amp;type=1&amp;theater">
          Return of The Ugly
         </a>
         at Chinnerys in Southend on sea (Dean Chalkley guest DJ session with SonnyScully Evans, and Dean from 1000 tons and more)
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         + Dean and Si Cheebas Black Cat will be on 20
         <sup>
          th
         </sup>
         April
         <a href="http://www.thesilverbullet.co.uk/listings/eventdetails/20-apr-13-black-cat-the-silver-bullet/">
          Black Cat at the Silver Bullet
         </a>
         Finsbury Park London (Si Cheeba, Dom Cater, Eli S Deutsch, Neil Barker, Elliot Gale (Dean will not be DJing at this Black Cat instead he'll be at the above for this one off, the rest of the collective will keep the dancefloor rolling)
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         A bit more about the nights:
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
          New Street Adventure:
         </span>
         Fresh from their signing to ACID JAZZ RECORDS and recording of their debut album, New Street Adventure explode back onto the scene at The Borderline Club on the 2
         <sup>
          nd
         </sup>
         April . This night will be BIG!! Black Catss Dean and Si Cheeba will be spinning a very eclectic selection after the band, expect Rhythm and Blues, Northern Soul, Funk , Latin Boogaloo and even a more good times Hip Hop angle to some of Mr. Cheebas selections.Black Cat is know for its cross pollination of styles , consistently great music that crosses genres and reaches to the outer limits, digging up killa tracks to the dancefloor. So get some rest this will be a night to remember
        </p>
        <p>
         It's 5 in advance:
         <a href="http://tinyurl.com/NSABORDERLINE">
          <strong>
           <br/>
          </strong>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
          DB Cohen album Launch Special Gig:
         </span>
         'Scratchcards and Wine' is the title of D.B.Cohen's excellent new album. For one night only all the players on the 'record' will play, it will be a sensational night . Black Cat DJ's Si Cheeba and Dean Chalkley are most honoured to provide exciting vinyl stimulation after D.B.Cohen and his band have performed so get down to the world famous TROUBADOUR club in Earls Court for a unique night.
        </p>
        <p>
         Only 8 on the door for this momentus evening.
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
          Return of The Ugly:
         </span>
         Dean guest DJ session with Sonny Scully Evans, and Dean from 1000 tons and more a Seaside special...Boss Reggae meets Soul and R&amp;B
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/february/blink_magazine_21_today">
         Blink Magazine : 21 today!!
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        02 February 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:02
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.blinkreflex.com/81">
          <img alt="blink pix" height="557" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/bc5bda34-6d3c-11e2-9386-fefd616b8533" width="398"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Previous
         <a href="http://www.blinkreflex.com/81">
          Blink
         </a>
         Covers shot by various photographers not Dean
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Blink Magazine samples" height="555" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/41e3e52c-6d36-11e2-a643-f23c91df768a" width="394"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Cover image of
         <a href="http://www.blinkreflex.com/81">
          BLINK
         </a>
         magazine issue 21 was shot by 
         <a href="http://www.williamcoupon.com/">
          William Coupon
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.wowsan.com/?tag=kim-aram">
          Kim Aram's
         </a>
         magazine
         <a href="http://www.blinkreflex.com/81">
          BLINK
         </a>
         goes on sale today. Limited to 500 copies this precious publication is unveiled, included in its ad free pages are the works of
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.danwen.com/web/">
          Danwen Xing
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.davidtitlow.com/">
          David Titlow
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://eliaswessel.com/">
          Elias Wessel
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://frieke.com/#!/">
          Frieke Janssens
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.julieblackmon.com/">
          Julie Blackmon
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://paulinasurys.co.uk/">
          Paulina Otylie Surys
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.williamcoupon.com/">
          William Coupon
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.bettinagenten.com/">
          Bettina Genten
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.charlotterutherford.com/">
          Charlotte Rutherford
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         and Dean of course...
        </p>
        <p>
         The magazine is highly respected and will only be available for a short period due to its limited numbers. So BLINK and you just might miss it...er hur...like that ?...
        </p>
        <p>
         Here some sample spreads from Dean and other photographers in the book:

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/january/foals_nme_26th_january_issue">
         FOALS: NME: 26th January Issue
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        25 January 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:01
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="foals for the nme" height="346" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/4795d20a-6728-11e2-88db-fefd616b8533" width="420"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         (Yannis from Foals)
        </p>
        <p>
         The current edition of the NME has a great piece on FOALS! The band has now well and truly shaken off the pigeon hole term of '
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Math_rock">
          Math Rock
         </a>
         '. With this great new Album. They say ' We wanted to have fun and write stuff that felt good from the waist down,' (Yannis Philippakis) well they have 100% done that. The single
         <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=qJ_PMvjmC6M">
          'Inhaler'
         </a>
         burst onto the scene and the album '
         <a href="http://holyfire.foals.co.uk/">
          Holy Fire
         </a>
         ' now follows...set for release on the 11th Feb 2013
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean Shot the band just after the Christmas break in West London (coincidentally in the same studio that he shot Paul Weller Miles Kane Noel Gallagher and Tim Burgess last year) The chaps were on good form and embraced the opportunity to make some very interesting photographs with Dean.
        </p>
        <p>
         You can get the digital version of the magazine
         <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/gb/app/nme-magazine/id530112491?mt=8">
          here
         </a>
         or get the Magazine from newsagents now.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="foals for the nme" height="365" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/604f69a0-6728-11e2-9469-f23c91df768a" width="392"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2013/january/foals_nme_26th_january_issue#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2013/january/foals_nme_26th_january_issue">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/january/scully_drops_into_shortlist_">
         'Scully' 'drops' into Shortlist
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        25 January 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  7:50
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         Here's a cool little thing that Shortlist wrote up on Sonny 'Scully' Evans. You'll of course know Scully as the main guy in
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/video/">
          Young Souls film
         </a>
         and he also featured in the photographic series of the same name. Here Scully gives a couple of hints on how to do a classic Northern Soul dance move , The Back Drop. Later this year our good friend Elaine Constantine will release her film Northern Soul - The Film we are very excited to see it and know that it will be a great piece of work.
        </p>
        <p>
         Right get practicing!!
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2013/january/cath_kidston_new_exciting_campaign">
         Cath Kidston new exciting Campaign
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        13 January 13
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:13
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://vimeo.com/57228952">
          <img alt="Cath Kidston home page" height="278" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/00891e98-5d6a-11e2-84f5-f23c91df768a" width="403"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Today elements of the new
         <a href="http://www.cathkidston.co.uk/">
          Cath Kidston Spring Summer 13 campaign
         </a>
         have been unveiled. The Sunday Times Business Magazine have featured a story on Kenny Wilson and his working relationship with Cath Kidston and the shareholders. It makes great reading!
        </p>
        <p>
         There is an immense lust for the product globally and the company is extremely keen to keep the brand fresh... Art Director
         <a href="http://www.anotherbeardeddesigner.com/index.php?/about-this-site/">
          Aaran Cawte
         </a>
         and Dean worked with the team at Cath Kidston to produce a startling new set of images that will filter out over the coming weeks.
        </p>
        <p>
         In the mean time here is a link to a short 'behind the scenes' film taken on set as the shoots were taking place, click
         <a href="http://vimeo.com/57228952">
          here
         </a>
         to view.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/december/merry_christmas_1">
         MERRY CHRISTMAS!!
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        24 December 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  5:16
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         It's been a big old year here at Chalkley Towers, a year of excitement and change. The ever evolving and rolling thing that is happening here has brought with it a change of location for us, a new agent (
         <a href="http://skinnydip.co.uk/">
          www.skinnydip.co.uk
         </a>
         ) and an explosion of new projects. Its a very productive time with lots of Photographic and Film shoots in the worlds of Fashion, Music and Culture. These include shoots for Fred Perry and Hush Puppies and lots of Bands and musicians here are just some of the many shoots Dean has done over the year,
         <a href="http://www.shortlist.com/entertainment/music/paul-mccartney">
          Paul McCartney
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.nme.com/ratemy/287202/60-years-of-nme/item/287226">
          Noel
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://www.nme.com/news/beady-eye/66323">
          Liam Gallagher
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.google.co.uk/imgres?imgurl=http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-d4c8liq-ONg/T4SLBcoeLdI/AAAAAAAAEjs/huw7Q0uMJ0E/s1600/MileKanePaulWellerMg100412.jpeg&amp;imgrefurl=http://paulwellernews.blogspot.com/2012/04/paul-weller-on-cover-of-this-weeks-nme.html&amp;h=368&amp;w=592&amp;sz=68&amp;tbnid=w4tEaeVhWuc5ZM:&amp;tbnh=90&amp;tbnw=145&amp;zoom=1&amp;usg=__TaUh49lFhM5z9SNVGk4sleom7CI=&amp;docid=8OSFxdvKJziI0M&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=SIbZUJGXEuat0QXbzICQBg&amp;ved=0CEEQ9QEwAw&amp;dur=339">
          Paul Weller, Miles Kane
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/november/on_the_road_with_jake_bugg_nme_cover_feature_171112">
          Jake Bugg
         </a>
         , Patti Smith, Alt-j,
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/october/bang_the_palma_violets_explode_onto_the_scene">
          Palma Violets
         </a>
         . Many of the projects will be released during next year including The Computers album cover (they have made a great new album), stuff inside the Palma Violets album (goes without saying this is one of the most anticipated albums of next year) and much much more. (oh happy 60th Birthday NME)
        </p>
        <p>
         On the Exhibition tip, the
         <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.co.uk/jason-holmes/the-royal-albert-hall-pre_b_1947369.html">
          Royal Albert Hall
         </a>
         , White Wall Space and Brighton's Hotel Pelirocco were all very notable. The former exhibition was accompanied by a gig curated by Dean, with Kitty Daisy and Lewis, New Street Adventure, Kieran Leonard.
        </p>
        <p>
         The creation of the Soul-a-trope was unique and very special (it may very well emerge again soon..) A special mention to
         <a href="http://www.thenewbritish.com/">
          The New British
         </a>
         , congratulations for getting one of the
         <a href="http://www.google.co.uk/imgres?imgurl=http://media.digitalphotogallery.com/fxyrcnkrfzfa/images/b79e296a-f01b-11e0-9cae-fefd616b8533/the_dogbones_02_website_image_sgjv_standard.jpg%3F20120228161427&amp;imgrefurl=http://www.deanchalkley.com/gallery/music/the_dogbones/&amp;h=900&amp;w=599&amp;sz=202&amp;tbnid=TebGEy_qec3c0M:&amp;tbnh=90&amp;tbnw=60&amp;zoom=1&amp;usg=__SOxWY1_TleLhOeiyrIfQR5DWVNc=&amp;docid=5vUhfhHcAufVsM&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=rYrZUJKpI8bM0QXVpIHQAw&amp;ved=0CGMQ9QEwCQ&amp;dur=469">
          best magazines
         </a>
         out of all time, the NME for keeping new music fresh and buzzing.
        </p>
        <p>
         ...So keep your eyes on the blog for more thrilling stuff, it might be photography, it might be film,it might be something else but it will be exciting! Thank you for checking out the blog we hope you enjoy the site and also hope you visit it regularly in the future for more news...MERRY CHRISTMAS TO YOU!! OH AND A HAPPY NEW YEAR!!
        </p>
        <p>
         If you are in the Essex area on the 29th December Dean will be Djing with
         <a href="https://twitter.com/BlackCatDJs">
          Black Cat DJ
         </a>
         buddy Si Cheeba at the
         <a href="http://radio.novalujon.com/category/soup-sessions/">
          Radio Novalujon
         </a>
         party at the
         <a href="http://www.railwayhotelsos.co.uk/">
          Railway Hotel
         </a>
         and if you are in London on the 31st December why not pop along to the 100 Club in Oxford Street London at the
         <a href="http://www.the100club.co.uk/gigs/new-years-eve-new-street-soul-club-100-club/">
          New Street Soul Club New Years Eve Party
         </a>
         . It'll be Northern Soul, Rhythm and Blues and Ska with a very Special live sets from The Spitfires and
         <a href="http://newstreetadventure.co.uk/">
          New Street Adventure
         </a>
         .
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/december/merry_christmas_1#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/december/merry_christmas_1">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>
      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/december/50_years_of_british_rock_exhibition_in_china">
         50 Years of British Rock Exhibition in China!
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        13 December 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 11:24
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="Rock Archive Exhibition" height="323" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/60094598-42bf-11e2-9e81-f23c91df768a" width="403"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Featured in this weeks
         <a href="http://www.britishcouncil.org/arts-uk-now.htm">
          UK NOW
         </a>
         (British Council for Arts &amp; Culture) is a special article on the
         <a href="http://www.britishcouncil.org/">
          British Council
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://www.rockarchive.com/">
          Rock Archive
         </a>
         s touring exhibition celebrating 50 years of British Rock!
        </p>
        <p>
         Amongst the 50 Iconic images, which included
         <a href="http://www.thebeatles.com/">
          The Beatles
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.rollingstones.com/">
          The Rolling Stones
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://www.coldplay.com/">
          Coldplay
         </a>
         was one of
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
          Dean
         </a>
         s very own shots of the contemporary national treasure
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adele_(singer)">
          Adele
         </a>
         . The Exhibition has been touring since May this year and was most recently shown at
         <a href="http://maps.google.co.uk/maps?sugexp=chrome,mod%3D18&amp;um=1&amp;ie=UTF-8&amp;q=Harbour+City,+Hong+Kong&amp;fb=1&amp;gl=uk&amp;hq=Harbour+City,+Hong+Kong&amp;hnear=Harbour+City,+Hong+Kong&amp;cid=0,0,10827396120794883254&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=Ps_FUNeYMsfY0QW_wYDIDw&amp;ved=0CIoBEPwSMAM">
          Harbour City, Hong Kong
         </a>
         from 12
         <sup>
          th
         </sup>
          18
         <sup>
          th
         </sup>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/november/in_france_with_altj_nme_cover_241112">
         In France with Alt-J NME Cover 24/11/12
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        27 November 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:51
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="alt-j" height="492" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/3d688d22-38d4-11e2-a69a-fefd616b8533" width="396"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         After
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/november/on_the_road_with_jake_bugg_nme_cover_feature_171112">
          last weeks on the road feature
         </a>
         on
         <a href="http://jakebugg.com/">
          Jake Bugg
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
          Dean Chalkley
         </a>
         's done it again and produced another cover and feature for
         <a href="http://www.nme.com/">
          NME magazine
         </a>
         but this time Dean travelled to France to join
         <a href="http://altjband.com/">
          Alt-J
         </a>
         on their European tour. The article explores the stratospheric rise of the band's debut and Mercury Award winning album '
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/An_Awesome_Wave">
          An Awesome Wave
         </a>
         '. The NME article was written by new NME hot shot writer
         <a href="http://wannabehacks.co.uk/2011/03/09/jenny-stevens-making-the-shift-from-political-to-arts-journalism/">
          Jenny Stevens
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         After catching the train from Kings Cross St Pancras, speeding over to Paris and then jumping on another train to the capital of Normandy the city of Evreux, Jenny interviewed the band whilst Dean and assistant Gideon Marshall set up an improvised 'studio' to shoot these and other unusual images of the band. They all then went to the bands gig that night where Dean shot the band in action. Check out the digital Edition of the magazine
         <a href="https://itunes.apple.com/gb/app/nme-magazine/id530112491?mt=8">
          here
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/november/young_souls_and_lookhear_at_the_royal_albert_hall">
         YOUNG SOULS and LOOK:HEAR at the Royal Albert Hall
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        27 November 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:44
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         Its been a big year for Deans exhibitions LOOK:HEAR and YOUNG SOULS.
        </p>
        <p>
         The LOOK:HEAR debut was in Leigh~on~Sea, Essex and YOUNG SOULS continued to ride its wave of success from release. With a show at the infamous Hotel Pelirocco in Brighton.
        </p>
        <p>
         In September the twocollectionscame together for the first time at one of Londons most Iconic and monumental venues the
         <a href="http://www.royalalberthall.com/search/?term=dean%20chalkley&amp;startD=2012-11-27&amp;endD=2013-11-27">
          Royal Albert Hall
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         The two collections complimented each other beautifully, one presenting us with a variety of Deans choice images from the vast pool of his Music Portraits, archives, containing both established (some of which have played at the venue) and new talent alike. The other being an exploration of the culture of Northern Soul, a music scene phenomenon focusing on a current burgeoning generation of young people who have immersed themselves into the music and culture that Dean himself, has collected and enjoyed since boyhood.
        </p>
        <p>
         The substantial photographic show at the Royal Albert hall was seen by 5000+ visitors PER NIGHT!! with a total residency of 5 weeks.
        </p>
        <p>
         Needless to say the show was a great success and reviewed and blogged about by the likes of
         <a href="http://www.itsnicethat.com/articles/dean-chalkley">
          Its Nice That
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://pymca.wordpress.com/2012/09/26/dean-chalkley-exhibition-at-the-royal-albert-hall/">
          PYMCA
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.theprintspace.co.uk/blog/dean-chalkley-look-hear/">
          The Print Space
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.co.uk/jason-holmes/the-royal-albert-hall-pre_b_1947369.html">
          The Huffington Post
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         Here are a few of the nice things that were said:
        </p>
        <p>
         it is about time the world got to see exactly what ten years of dedication looks like.  Its Nice That
        </p>
        <p>
         it is immediately evident that this self-effacing Southend-on-Sea-born man is at one with his craft, ostensibly picking up from where David Bailey and Terry O'Neill have left off.  Huffington Post
        </p>
        <p>
         *As a side note whilst the exhibition adorned the walls of the Royal Albert Hall many events took place at the world famous and iconic venue, The Beach Boys were amongst the performances and it was also the world Premiere of 'Skyfall' the latest James Bond film....
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/november/young_souls_and_lookhear_at_the_royal_albert_hall#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/november/young_souls_and_lookhear_at_the_royal_albert_hall">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/october/london_calling_oz_">
         London Calling Oz!
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        19 October 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:56
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         Eminent writter and filmmaker
         <a href="http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0937017/">
          Simon Witter
         </a>
         has produced aFantastic documentary series entitled
         <em>
          London Calling: The Untold Story Of British Pop.
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         The series started in Australia last week on the Arts and Culture Channel
         <em>
          <a href="http://www.studiotv.com.au/highlights/london-calling/">
           Studio
          </a>
          . There are 4 programmes in the series each approx. 1 hour long.
         </em>
         Dean features in the second programme of the series 'Every Picture Tells A Story', it is due to be aired on Tuesday 23rd October 2012.
        </p>
        <p>
         Just before Christmas last year Dean was Interviewed by Simon Witterforthe programme. It's firstbroadcast came on
         <a href="http://www.arte.tv/de/london-calling/6732310.html">
          ARTE, (the European Arts and Culture Channel)
         </a>
         earlier this year amidst the London centric summer of Jubilee celebrations and Olympic triumph. The Series Screened on UK T.V.'s via the Sky Arts Channel around 3 weeks ago and now Australia is delighting in the show.
        </p>
        <p>
         <em>
          London Calling: The Untold Story Of British Pop
         </em>
         focuses on the British Pop/Rock culture as well as celebrating its relationship within other artistic disciplines. Dean features alongside legendary photographers
         <a href="http://www.jillfurmanovsky.com/">
          Jill Furmanovsky
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pennie_Smith">
          Pennie Smith
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://www.mankowitz.com/">
          Gered Mankowitz
         </a>
         , Writers
         <a href="http://www.jonsavage.com/">
          Jon Savage
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/profile/paulmorley">
          Paul Morley
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boy_George">
          Boy George
         </a>
         and managers
         <a href="http://www.simonnapierbell.com/">
          Simon Napier-Bell
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrew_Loog_Oldham">
          Andrew Loog Oldham
         </a>
         as well as artist/musician
         <a href="https://twitter.com/FredDeakin">
          Fred Deakin
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <p>
         Interviewed at his North London Studio, Dean talked at length about the current scene and the nurturing of new talent, offering a contrast to his peers more historical insights.
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean also invited the the London Calling cameras along to
         <a href="http://www.shoreditchstudios.com/">
          Shorditch Studios
         </a>
         inLondon to hang out and document a live shoot in progress with the young and soulful band
         <a href="http://newstreetadventure.co.uk/">
          <em>
           New Street Adventure
          </em>
         </a>
         . Dean has affiliated himself with New Street Adventure, inviting them to play at his immensely well-attended and enjoyed opening parties/private views for his latest exhibition 
         <a href="http://www.itsnicethat.com/articles/dean-chalkley">
          LOOK. HEAR
         </a>
          shown in Leigh-on-Seaat the beginning of the year and now currently resideing along side YOUNG SOULS (another exhibition by Dean) at the
         <a href="http://waiting.royalalberthall.com/">
          Royal Albert Hall
         </a>
         , London until the 26th October 2012.
        </p>
        <p>
         Here's a taster of the series.
        </p>
        <p>
         <iframe frameborder="0" height="315" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/3NKfXNDK1BQ" width="560">
         </iframe>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/october/london_calling_oz_#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/october/london_calling_oz_">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/october/muse_nme">
         Muse - NME
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        19 October 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:50
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         This week, Dean's cover shot of
         <a href="http://muse.mu/">
          Muse
         </a>
         for
         <a href="http://www.nme.com/magazine">
          NME
         </a>
         graces News-stands across the country. Dean shot Muse last Thursday during their rehearsals (yes Rehersals! they actually took over Wembley Arena to reherse in!!) for their 2nd Law tour promoting their latest album of the same name.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Muse NME cover 2012" height="497" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/7a28bbaa-19db-11e2-9f58-f23c91df768a" width="402"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The interview with Tom Howard gives NMEs readers a behind-the-scenes look into the bands maddest tour ever, with in depth descriptions of the astonishly impressive set designed by Matt Bellamy himself.
        </p>
        <p>
         Muses 6
         <sup>
          th
         </sup>
         studio album '2
         <sup>
          nd
         </sup>
         Law' was given a very credible 8/10 in NME and, as the band informed Dean on the day of the shoot, that the album artwork is an illustration of the human brains intricate circuitry system, where the connections of how we process information has been represented in a colour coded graphic...Which is pretty cool.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/october/open_day_at_the_royal_albert_hall_saturday_6th_october">
         Open Day at the Royal Albert Hall: Saturday 6th October
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        05 October 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  5:01
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         Dean's 'Young Souls' and 'Look.Hear' exhibitions remain up in the Royal Albert Hall until the 26th October, but this Saturday (6th October) will be the final Public Open Day.
        </p>
        <p>
         In other words this will be the last time you can just roll into the Royal Albert Hall off the street unless you are going to see a performance or on a guided tour. So, if you can make it along between 10am -3pm on Saturday it is the ideal time to see the work. We have heard that people have just arrived at the venue outside of the Public Open Days and have still been allowed to view the exhibitions but entry cannot be guaranteed, it is at the managements discretion. Click
         <a href="http://www.royalalberthall.com/reflect/dean-chalkley.aspx">
          here
         </a>
         for Royal Albert Hall Details.
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/october/nice">
         Nice!!!..........
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        02 October 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  3:43
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         'It's Nice That' is The Barometer for what's hot and what's not.
        </p>
        <p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/september/royal_albert_hall_exhibition_runs_until_the_26th_october">
         Royal Albert Hall Exhibition Runs until the 26th October
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        29 September 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:47
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         Already thousands of visitors to the Royal Albert Hall haveseen the LOOK.HEAR and YOUNG SOULS exhibitions.
        </p>
        <p>
         The iconic venuepresent concerts virtually every night, on average 5000 people come through the doors and view the exhibitions before settling down to see their particular show.
        </p>
        <p>
         The exhibitions are not just for audiences of the Albert Hall though. 'open to the public days' allow people to just walk in off the street and see the work too. There have been a few of these already, the next will be the 6th October. The "open to the public days'' are free to enter between 10am-3pm.
        </p>
        <p>
         ...Hope you can make it along!
        </p>
        <p>
         Click
         <a href="http://www.royalalberthall.com">
          here
         </a>
         for Royal Albert Hall details.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/september/royal_albert_hall_lookhear_and_young_souls_exhibitions_announced_">
         Royal Albert Hall: LOOK.HEAR and YOUNG SOULS Exhibitions Announced
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        07 September 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:02
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="royal albert hall official picture" height="214" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/cc2f8d98-f875-11e1-86cd-fefd616b8533" width="285"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         RAH picture  Marcus Ginns
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          The Royal Albert Hall presents Dean Chalkley
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Thursday 20th September - Friday 26th October 2012
         </strong>
         <a href="http://life.royalalberthall.com/2012/09/dean-chalkley-lookhear-exhibition/">
          <span>
           <strong>
            NOW ON!!!!
           </strong>
          </span>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Dean is exhibiting both LOOK.HEAR and YOUNG SOULS exhibitions at the iconic and legendary Royal Albert Hall.
        </p>
        <p>
         LOOK.HEAR is a collection of large fine art photographic prints depicting many of the heroes and heroines of the music scene. Dean has shot the likes of Florence (and the machine) Welch, Kasabian, The Kills, Paul Weller, Ian Brown, Noel and Liam Gallagher all these and many more appear in the LOOK.HEAR exhibition.
        </p>
        <p>
         YOUNG SOULS is a contemporary study of kids that are into the Northern Soul scene; originally published in the uber stylish 125 Magazine, this collection of prints is a perfect accompaniment to LOOK.HEAR further reflecting Dean's interest in the transferenceof music into a culture.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Both Shows run side by side, so a substantial photographic show awaits you.
        </p>
        <p>
         Virtually every night audiences of 5000+ stream through the doors of the Royal Albert Hall so it's fair to say the exhibition will be viewed by a vast amount of people over it's run.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          GO SEE IT FOR FREE!
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         There are also free entry public open days, a perfect time to pop down if you have no plans to actually see a show at the venue.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Public Open Days:
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         Saturday 22 September 2012, 10am  3pm
        </p>
        <p>
         Sunday  23 September 2012, 10am  3pm
        </p>
        <p>
         Saturday 29 September 2012, 10am  3pm
        </p>
        <p>
         Saturday 06 October   2012, 10am  3pm
        </p>
        <p>
         Special Exhibition Party:
        </p>
        <p>
         There will be a special private view party too,...hush hush at the moment entry by special invite only but there may be a few spaces available through this news blog and /or twitter (nitzerdc) so keep an eye on these information streams over the coming weeks.
        </p>
        <p>
         How exciting. for more information click
         <a href="http://www.royalalberthall.com/reflect/dean-chalkley.aspx">
          here
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/september/royal_albert_hall_lookhear_and_young_souls_exhibitions_announced_#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/september/royal_albert_hall_lookhear_and_young_souls_exhibitions_announced_">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/september/the_van_dor_awards_young_souls_shortlisted">
         The VAN d'OR Awards - Young Souls Shortlisted
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        06 September 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 11:24
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="Van d'or poster" height="239" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/e6fd193e-f86f-11e1-aa7b-f23c91df768a" width="400"/>
        </p>
        <p class="p1">
         The awards night will be celebrating the brightestlights in film, animation and motion design and rewarding those shortlistedin 15 categories including Best Feature, Best Director, Best Animation, BestActor &amp; Actress and the coveted Van d'Or for Best Film.Among the judges on this year's
         <strong>
          Van d'Or Jury
         </strong>
         are award-winning directorGurinder Chadha OBE (Bend It Like Beckham, Bride and Prejudice),Oscar-nominated producer Samantha Waite (Wish 143), Editorial Director ofLittle White Lies Matt Bochenski and a host of industry figures from across the film &amp;media sphere.The 2012 Jury will make a decision based on a clearly defined set ofcriteria. The awards themselves will be hosted at Hackney House on the 14th September. The
         <a href="http://www.hackneyhouse.org/">
          Hackney House
         </a>
         is a sizzlingnew Olympic pop-up venue in the heart of London's creative hub of Shoreditch.
         <span class="s1">
          How exciting.
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="p1">
         <span class="s1">
          Come on Young Souls !!
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="p1">
         <strong>
          Update
         </strong>
         : Well Young Souls didn't win sadly, but... the film was actually nominated for 2 awards. Firstly the 'Best Music Based Film' and the second nomination for 'Best Cinematography' so we were all extremely pleased (especially Benoit Soler our brilliant Cinematographer) that the film was shortlisted in both categories. So great news! The event was great and the Cannes in a Van crew made a great party and ceremony.
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/september/the_van_dor_awards_young_souls_shortlisted#comments">

         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>

       </h2>

       </h3>

       <div class="content">

         <img alt="Matt Skelhon" height="564" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/1df7cc9e-f33f-11e1-a736-fefd616b8533" width="398"/>

         </a>
         will take aim and start shooting for Gold at 9am today. He's a great marksman, in Beijing Matt won Gold and we are of course hoping that this games are equally as fruitful.Dean photographed Matt in his back garden as well as in his 'Model Making Den' a short while before the games. You can't miss Matt with his shock of blue hair and piecing eyes, he is a great character and an inspiration. Click

          here
         </a>
         to read all about it. There is one thing Matt has lost however and that's his blue hair, it's gone, shaved off, vanished.

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/august/kieran_leonard_releases_his_debut_album">
         Kieran Leonard releases his debut album
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        29 August 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  6:54
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="kieran Leonard" height="430" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/bc762dc0-f1ff-11e1-abc4-f23c91df768a" width="402"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Kieran Leonard is a name you will become very familiar with in the future.
        </p>
        <p>
         He has just released his first and very accomplished album entitled 'Out Of Work Astronaut'.
        </p>
        <p>
         Kieran is particularly known for his poetical song writing and compelling live performances. There is a clear social and political awareness in his writing with an abundance of literary and cultural references. He has had critical comparisons to
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bob_Dylan">
          Bob Dylan
         </a>
         ,
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kurt_Cobain">
          Kurt Cobain
         </a>
         and
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leonard_Cohen">
          Leonard Cohen
         </a>
         .In early 2011 his first single 'Jerusalem' was used in the soundtrack for
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ridley_Scott">
          Ridley Scott
         </a>
         's latest documentary film '
         <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Life_in_a_Day_%282011_film%29">
          Life in a Day
         </a>
         '.
        </p>
        <p>
         In Spring 2012 Kieran established his 'The Chance To Fail Foundation' as a response to the London riots and the closure of community youth centres. The foundation for 12-16 year olds aims to teach the craft of songwriting and recording music as a constructive creative outlet, and a way of empowering disadvantaged young people in the capital.
        </p>
        <p>
         Here are a few videos:
         <a href="http://youtu.be/D_u6ORpRc30">
          1
         </a>
         <a href="http://youtu.be/gsbT6ZtQEbg">
          2
         </a>
         <a href="http://youtu.be/i_xUE_LK66A">
          3
         </a>
         <a href="http://youtu.be/UsoRMpe_LuA">
          4
         </a>
         <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=zaB_qpgHiJw">
          5
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          HERE IS A VERY SPECIAL INVITE Album Launch Party :
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         FRIDAY 31ST AUGUST 20128PM FREE ENTRY. FREE COCKTAILS.
        </p>
        <p>
         THE GOPHER HOLE
        </p>
        <p>
         350-354 Old St, EC1V 9NQ
        </p>
        <p>
         RSVP FACEBOOK
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="https://www.facebook.com/events/396636053732001/">
          https://www.facebook.com/events/396636053732001/
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/august/kieran_leonard_releases_his_debut_album#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/august/kieran_leonard_releases_his_debut_album">
