       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/august/mariellas_fear_of_the_dark_observer_magazine_today">
         Mariella's Fear of the Dark: Observer Magazine today.
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        26 August 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:10
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="Mariella Frostrup's Fear of the Dark" height="488" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/912b1a82-ed49-11e1-b308-f23c91df768a" width="401"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         When Mariella Frostrup mentioned she was frightened of the dark in one of her agony aunt colomns, her comments really caught the public's attention. She had so many letters from people who shared this phobia she decided to look more deeply into her 'Night Terrors'.
        </p>

        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/august/behind_the_lines_nme_25_august">
         Behind The Lines: NME 25 August
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        24 August 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  7:55
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="nme behind the lines" height="347" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/e1f463a8-edf1-11e1-b9aa-f23c91df768a" width="529"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The NME is celebrating its 60th anniversary. There are a whole series offeatures emerging that highlight the importance of the magazine and it's enduring influence.
        </p>
        <p>
         BEHIND THE LINES is a series of rare interviews with the photographers who have created some of the most iconic photographs that have appeared in the magazine over the years. This week the magazine talks to Dean about his quite surreal shot of the White Stripes. 'Big Bang..' gives you a clue to one of the things discussed, you'll have to pop out and get the magazine to read all about it all though (or stand in the news agents and pretend you're going to buy one...).There's lots more in the Magazine beside this feature of course. It's a kind of Vaccines meets Reading/Leeds Festival special so tons ofnews aboutfreshup and coming music as well as what to expect this weekend at the festival. Go on! Rush out and scoop up a copy...You know you want to...
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/august/kentish_town_relaxed_and_dapper">
         Kentish Town Relaxed and Dapper
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        10 August 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:42
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="dapper Italian chap in Kentish Town" height="592" src="http://media.digitalphotogallery.com/fxyrcnkrfzfa/images/98254cb8-e330-11e1-9f34-fefd616b8533/old_italian_guy_kentish_town01_blog_image.jpg" width="401"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         How amazing does this guy look?... This dapper gent was photographed in Kentish Town by Dean this week. Dean said 'I thought he looked so great and totally authentic. This chap was not into 'The Look'. He was The Look, The Look was his!! I approached this just over 5 foot fellow and asked him if I could take his picture. He seemed surprised that anyone would want to, but in a strong Italian accent agreed. He also explained that his Daughter was a Photographer, if you are out there let me know who you are and please compliment your father on his appearance... Anyway after a few moments he was gone, into the station and on his way... Maybe he was over in London for the Olympics ?... Maybe I'll never know'.
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/july/paul_mccartney_cover_feature_of_the_shortlist_magazine_olympic_special">
         Paul McCartney : Cover Feature of the Shortlist Magazine Olympic Special
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        26 July 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  7:28
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Untitled" height="576" src="http://permanent.media.digitalphotogallery.com/images/57c69c40-d74f-11e1-89e7-fefd616b8533" width="403"/>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         The Olympics have well and truly arrived in London!! Everywhere you look theres evidence of this massive sporting occasion.
        </p>
        <p>
         The next few weeks will be fun in old London Town, even more people people hustling and bustling on the tubes, lots of people smiling and talking with passes round their necks excitedly dashing towards Stratford, etc etc.. Its a gigantic event and London seems to be ready!!.
        </p>
        <p>
         Shortlist Magazine asked Dean to do a session with Sir Paul McCartney for the cover of the Olympic Special... Dean jumped at offer.
        </p>
        <p>
         The Olympic Special Shortlist Feature includes the cover and 4 pages inside the Magazine. There are several photographs and the Q&amp;A asks Sir Paul a raft of questions both musical and sporting. 'Do you have any concept of your status and influence?..' and 'What's your sporting pedigree like?' are just two examples it's a good read. There is no doubt Sir Paul is still having a great time enjoying life and excited about stuff!!
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Oh and one final thing he is a total Legend isn't he!..
        </p>

        </a>

          </a>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/june/the_soulatrope_behind_the_scenes_story">
         The Soul-a-Trope (behind the scenes story)
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        24 June 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:56
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
          <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-OhxFi2mzv5M/T-cXwG2y1PI/AAAAAAAAAO0/wkchzJcXi8M/s1600/DSCF0908h.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-OhxFi2mzv5M/T-cXwG2y1PI/AAAAAAAAAO0/wkchzJcXi8M/s640/DSCF0908h.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          This image shows a prototype component of Deans installation known as the Soul-a-Trope. The Soul-a-Trope (???) I hear you say... Havent you heard about the Soul-a-Trope? Well in many ways it represents an extension of Dean's visual repertoire. It's not strictly photography or strictly film, it's an amalgamation of both but presented as a gallery piece. Only seen once so far in public. Viewers responses were great, some could not comprehend it or factum out exactly what they were looking at...but all liked it and found it stimulating and engaging.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The Installation will appear again soon so please watch this space.
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/june/the_soulatrope_behind_the_scenes_story#comments">

        </a>

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/june/krissi_murison_nme_editor_leaves">
         Krissi Murison NME Editor Leaves
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        24 June 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:49
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7K_YxIbLX9I/T-cSiRrip7I/AAAAAAAAAOo/IU4AhW9NIho/s1600/dscr0956h.jpg">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7K_YxIbLX9I/T-cSiRrip7I/AAAAAAAAAOo/IU4AhW9NIho/s320/dscr0956h.jpg"/>
         </a>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         Friday 22nd June 2012 was the last day of Krissi Murison's Editorship at the NME. This is a picture from her leaving 'Do'. The magazine always make a spoof cover for leaving presents.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         Krissi was appointed in 2009, she became the first female editor the NME. Previously Krissi had worked for the title as a journalist and then for a brief period taken a position at Nylon Magazine. Her passion knowledge and charisma all made her the ideal choice to become the New Editor when Conor McNicholas the former Editor left.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         Whilst at the helm Krissi commissioned many inspirational features none more controversial than a
         <a href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/media/organgrinder/2009/dec/15/simon-cowell-v-nme">
          Christmas Simon Cowell story
         </a>
         . This was a great subversive moment that devided opinion, created debate and generally stirred things up.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         Dean Says "Krissi is first and foremost a lovely individual, a person who truly cares about music. She is not frightened stick her hand in the hornets nest if it means pulling out a good story. She kept the NME at the cutting edge of things as well as reflecting the heritage of the music world. So good luck Krissi in your next job it was an absolute pleasure working with you."
         <br/>
         <br/>
         Krissi will join The Sunday Times Magazine as Features Editor. The new Editor of the NME will be Mike Williams he has been Deputy Editor since July 2011 perfectly positioned to get stuck in and take the magazine into the future.
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/june/krissi_murison_nme_editor_leaves#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/june/krissi_murison_nme_editor_leaves">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/june/winner_of_the_harrods_fathersdaymemories_competition_on_twitter">
         Winner of the Harrods #FathersDayMemories Competition on Twitter
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        15 June 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:53
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uchsg5MKjqo/T99jWvO9UnI/AAAAAAAAAOc/Thi3GBsEzpM/s1600/original.gif">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uchsg5MKjqo/T99jWvO9UnI/AAAAAAAAAOc/Thi3GBsEzpM/s320/original.gif"/>
         </a>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
          Copyright @Sallyann17
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The Harrods Fathers Day Memories Competition was announced through Twitter on Friday 15th June. People sent lots of great images from their childhood with their Dads. So many of the pictures showed great humour, fondness and the special bond that is between kids and their Fathers. But after a very enjoyable editing process Dean settled on one image as the winner..This is how the winning image was announced on twitter
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Congratulations
          <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/Sallyann17">
           @Sallyann17
          </a>
          Congratulations Sallyann - you will receive this
          <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/Fujifilm_UK">
           @Fujifilm_UK
          </a>
          X100 Black Premium Edition camera -
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/Sallyann17">
           @Sallyann17
          </a>
          The reason
          <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/nitzerdc">
           @nitzerdc
          </a>
          chose your photograph was because he thought it really showed a very protective love.
          <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/search/%23FathersDayMemories">
           #FathersDayMemories
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Dean said, "There were some great pictures sent through, some really funny ones, some odd ones and loads of cute ones too of course. It was a very close decision and difficult to judge one emotion against another but I think the winning image really shows a very protective love, so congratulations to the winner. Everybody who entered took time to send their great memories through, so thanks for the great response it looks like you all had brilliant childhood memories with your fathers and these photographs will always remind you of those great times..Thank you for sharing them with us."
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>

        </a>

        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        01 June 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:07
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          It is said that a photograph is worth a thousand words. So with that in mind, Harrods are launching their
          <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/search/%23FathersDayMemories">
           #FathersDayMemories
          </a>
          competition.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Simply tweet them a childhood photo of you and your father with the hashtag
          <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/search/%23FathersDayMemories">
           #FathersDayMemories
          </a>
          . Here are some examples
          <a href="http://ow.ly/i/FkYs">
           http://ow.ly/i/FkYs
          </a>

           @nitzerdc
          </a>
          and receive a
          <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/Fujifilm_UK">
           @Fujifilm_UK
          </a>
          X100 Black Premium Edition camera -
          <a href="http://t.co/lQ8a624O">
           http://ow.ly/i/FkZk
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          You have until Thursday 14th June to tweet them your photos ASAP. The winner will be announced on Friday 15th June. Good luck...and get sending
          <br/>
          <br/>
          I would also say go for the creative pictures the ones that tell a story, that have mood atmosphere fun etc etc...
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Here are the simple instructions to enter the competition:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Simply tweet
          <a href="https://twitter.com/#!/harrods">
           @Harrods
          </a>
          a childhood photo of you and your father with the hashtag #FathersDayMemories good luck ... oh and the #FathersDayMemories is important. Don't forget to include it!

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/may/from_coast_to_coast">
         From Coast to Coast
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        25 May 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:41
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          From Margate in the UK to Seattle in the USA. This weekend is another big one for Young Souls.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          1-6-12
          <br/>
          Feed Back from the SIFF was that the Screening in the Seattle Uptown Theatre on Sunday 27th was sold out ... a full house !! Brilliant that the collection of 7 films from the UK they presented captured the audiences attention and got such a great turn responce.
          <br/>
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          27-5-12
          <br/>
          SOUL TOWN
          <br/>
          Westcoast-Margate
          <br/>
          The Famous seaside town of Margate is holding a very special event known as
          <a href="http://www.facebook.com/events/437392559621488/">
           SOUL TOWN
          </a>
          . It's a Celebration of Great British Youth Culture and Heritage. Young Souls will be included in a programme of short films made by Dean. In addition there will be 2 other short clip films on the bill by 'Hemingway Designs for Hush Puppies'. The films will be projected in the 'SOUL CINEMA', at the Westcoast Venue, between 3pm to 9pm. The whole event runs from 1pm until 11pm. It will be a great weekend in Margate the Sun will be shining and the ice cream flowing, so little better places to hang out, dance to Soul music and pop into the cinema for some shade and catch the films.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          27-5-12
          <br/>
          SIFF (Seattle International Film Festival)
          <br/>
          Cinema Uptown - Seattle
          <br/>
          SIFF's mission is to create experiences that bringspeople together to discover extraordinary films from around the world. It is through the art of cinema that they foster a community that is more informed, aware, and alive. This is why the festival thought that it was important to have Young Souls included in their programme. You can find out more about SIFF and what is America's largest film festival by clicking
          <a href="http://www.siff.net/index.aspx">
           here
          </a>
          . Young Souls will screen on Sunday so if you are in the area pop along and cheer the film on!..More later about this wonderful film festival so watch this space.
         </span>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <br/>
        </div>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/may/deans_talk_at_brentwood_ursuline_convent_high_school">
         Dean's Talk at Brentwood Ursuline Convent High School
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        21 May 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:44
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Last Thursday (17th May),
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean
          </a>
          paid a visit to
          <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brentwood_Ursuline_Convent_High_School">
           Brentwood Ursuline Convent High School for Girls
          </a>
          to give a talk to the year 12 and 13 Photography students.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The talk took place in the library. Dean showed the students a selection of photographs he had taken throughout his career, from early collage work to the present day. The talk was then followed by a Q &amp; A with lots of questions from the eager students and a short portfolio review, where the girls showed some very promising work.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HZ9KjrIsJIU/T7ofHK1GswI/AAAAAAAAAOQ/JOsrODTqbzE/s1600/photo%5B2%5D2.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HZ9KjrIsJIU/T7ofHK1GswI/AAAAAAAAAOQ/JOsrODTqbzE/s400/photo%5B2%5D2.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Heres a picture of some hand carved figurines of the Madonna and Child and the Sacred Heart contained within the doors off a busy hallway in the 112 year old convent school.
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/may/a_busy_time">
         A Busy Time...
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        18 May 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:48
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
          <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FKpYvFL92-U/T7aHU0W5h6I/AAAAAAAAANg/FGavarVhbgs/s1600/YoungSoulsSouthendwhite+redtype.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FKpYvFL92-U/T7aHU0W5h6I/AAAAAAAAANg/FGavarVhbgs/s640/YoungSoulsSouthendwhite+redtype.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          12-5-12
          <a href="http://www.southendfilmfestival.com/2012_Festival/Film_Schedule/Saturday_12th_May/saturday_12th_may.html">
           Almost Grown Cellar Cinema Club
          </a>
          <br/>
          Dean created this 'Happening' in the famous basement of The Royal Hotel in Southend-on-Sea Essex UK. The 'Cellar Cinema Club' was a great link up, an amalgamation of film and music on a weekend that brought thousands of Scooterists to the sunny Essex coastal town of Southend-on-Sea. 'Almost Grown' is one of Essex's foremost Mod and Soul clubs and they organized a whole 'Weekender' of club nights. Dean laced together the 'Cellar Cinema' daytime idea hooking up Almost Grown with the Southend Film Festival, securing a brilliant opportunity to screen Young Souls to Film lovers and lovers of Soul music too. It was the last event in the programme on the Southend Film Festival fringe schedule.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The happening was multi-faceted incorporating 6 exciting and different elements to stimulate all the senses The Almost Grown Cellar Cinema Club comprised of:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          1. Young Souls, screened on the hour every hour between 4pm to 8pm.
          <br/>
          2. 'In Orbit : Periphery of Young Souls', a brand new just under 3 minute film of unseen footage taken from the edge of the Young Souls main filming.
          <br/>
          3. 'Bodies Brut &amp; Talc' and Odor Installation
          <br/>
          4. '6 DJ's' playing music of the style and period.
          <br/>
          5. 'Scully's Car from the film Young Souls ' presented as a static display
          <br/>
          6. 'Soulatrope' this very special never seen before installation that brings together dancing, vinyl, atmosphere and aesthetic, in a surreal manner.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Between 3pm - 8pm on Saturday 12th May 2012
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The basement of the Royal Hotel became a very unique happening.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ruH4aE5YA30/T7aJSaBsNTI/AAAAAAAAANo/oeC9l37HY7s/s1600/090512DeanChalkley-290x290.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ruH4aE5YA30/T7aJSaBsNTI/AAAAAAAAANo/oeC9l37HY7s/s1600/090512DeanChalkley-290x290.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          9-5-12 Radio Shows
          <br/>
          Dean guests and then presents on 2 radio broadcasts,
          <a href="http://radio.novalujon.com/09-05-12-dean-chalkley/">
           The Soup Sessions on Radio.Novalujon
          </a>
          and
          <a href="http://www.mixcloud.com/robert-messer/dean-chalkley-guests-on-soulful-porridge-with-rob-messer-9th-may-2012/">
           Rob Messer's 'Soul Porridge'
          </a>
          on Stomp Radio.
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/may/a_busy_time#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/may/a_busy_time">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/may/young_souls_wins_at_southend_film_festival">
         Young Souls wins at Southend Film Festival
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        10 May 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  2:23
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Jdtj9Fn78w4/T6vo8814BNI/AAAAAAAAANU/AtKiV0CoXLc/s1600/IMG_4250edweb.jpg">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Jdtj9Fn78w4/T6vo8814BNI/AAAAAAAAANU/AtKiV0CoXLc/s640/IMG_4250edweb.jpg"/>
         </a>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Copyright  Nicola Jane 2012
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          On Tuesday this week
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean
          </a>
          attended the
          <a href="http://www.southendfilmfestival.com/">
           Southend Film Festival
          </a>
          Awards ceremony along with
          <a href="http://www.imdb.com/name/nm4671205/">
           Sonny "Scully" Evans
          </a>
          (who stared as the lead in the film) where his short film
          <a href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt2058140/">
           YOUNG SOULS
          </a>
          had been nominated for Best Short Film in the Music category. We are very pleased to announce that Young Souls won in that category! This is the 2nd award that YOUNG SOULS has secured since it was released back in July 2011, winning in the moving image category of
          <a href="http://www.creativereview.co.uk/cr-blog/2011/november/photography-annual-motion-category">
           Creative Review's Photography Annual
          </a>
          . Young Souls has been very popular on the film festival circuit having already been shown at the
          <a href="http://shortfilms.org.uk/">
           London Short Film Festival
          </a>
          and
          <a href="http://www.cinequest.org/event_view.php?eid=1677">
           Cinequest
          </a>
          , USA and will be shown at the Seattle International Film Festival at the end of May. You can now keep up-to-date with the film by following
          <a href="http://twitter.com/#!/YOUNG_SOULS">
           YOUNG SOULS on twitter
          </a>
          and subscribe to the
          <a href="http://www.facebook.com/youngsoulsfilm">
           YOUNG SOULS page on Facebook
          </a>
          .
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/may/young_souls_wins_at_southend_film_festival#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/may/young_souls_wins_at_southend_film_festival">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        04 May 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  2:43
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Tune in on Wednesday 9th May, at 9pm for
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean Chalkley
          </a>
          's first live solo broadcast on
          <a href="http://www.jazzdj.co.uk/">
           Nova Lujon.com
          </a>
          's "Soup Sessions".
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-S9qc6U6C5qE/T6PNFcwyKdI/AAAAAAAAANI/ur4AyYaOioE/s1600/090512DeanChalkley.jpeg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-S9qc6U6C5qE/T6PNFcwyKdI/AAAAAAAAANI/ur4AyYaOioE/s400/090512DeanChalkley.jpeg"/>

          <br/>

          Dean will be spinning you up some vinyl delights of Northern Soul, R&amp;B and more! Join them for an audio adventure presented to you in full stereo sound live from 9pm (GMT+1)! NOT TO BE MISSED!

          "I'm really looking forward to getting down to Nova Lujon towers with my car stacked full of vinyl to delight and excite the Internet airwaves." -

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/may/southend_film_festival">
         Southend Film Festival
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        02 May 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  2:45
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Currently all the entries for the
          <a href="http://www.southendfilmfestival.com/index.html">
           Southend Film Festival Short Film
          </a>
          Competition are being judged by actor
          <a href="http://www.imdb.com/name/nm0072610/">
           Perry Benson
          </a>
          . The awards ceremony will take place at the
          <a href="http://www.parkinn.co.uk/hotel-southendonsea">
           Park Inn Palace Hotel
          </a>
          on Tuesday 8th May and starts at 7pm. Clips from all the entered films will be played and the winning Films will be screened in their entirety. It will be a great night out at the Park Inn Palace and all are welcome it is free entry so come down and support the festival and see some good stuff...come on!!!!
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/may/young_souls_to_be_shown_at_seattle_international_film_festival_2012">
         Young Souls to be shown at Seattle International Film Festival 2012
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        01 May 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  2:51
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-y35nrShWNLg/T6ANIlFQ32I/AAAAAAAAAM8/2jmX6vlYIfY/s1600/SIFF2012_selectionlaurels.jpg">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-y35nrShWNLg/T6ANIlFQ32I/AAAAAAAAAM8/2jmX6vlYIfY/s400/SIFF2012_selectionlaurels.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          We are extremely pleased to announce that
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean Chalkley
          </a>
          s short film
          <a href="http://www.facebook.com/youngsoulsfilm">
           YOUNG SOULS
          </a>
          will be included in the highly prestigious
          <a href="http://www.siff.net/">
           Seattle International Film Festival
          </a>
          (SIFF) in Washington, USA!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          SIFF runs from May 17th until June 10th and is the largest and most well attended film festival in the United States with 160,000 attendees expected in 2012. SIFF is also a recognised
          <a href="http://oscar.go.com/">
           Oscar
          </a>
          nominating Festival in the categories of Best Short Film and Best Animated Short Film!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.facebook.com/youngsoulsfilm">
           YOUNG SOULS
          </a>
          s will be screened at the
          <a href="http://www.siff.net/">
           SIFF
          </a>
          s Uptown Theatre on Sunday 27th May as apart of the ShortsFest Weekend
         </span>
         <div>
          <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
           <br/>
           Heres the 2012 Trailer for the Festival.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           "The Seattle International Film Festival is a BIG DEAL!!! How amazing that Young Souls has been selected. It means a hell of a lot to me. Young Souls is now getting out there, audiences are getting a kick out of it and being turned on whether they are knowing of the culture or not. The SIFF is a highly prestigious Film Festival and the largest in the USA, so the film will reach out in a physical way as never before. Young Souls is amongst incredible company just look at the festivals programme.. I can't wait for the audience to come through the door to settle down, for the lights to dim and then to start tapping their feet and watching the story of Young Souls unfold." - Dean Chalkley (2012)
          </span>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/may/young_souls_to_be_shown_at_seattle_international_film_festival_2012#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/may/young_souls_to_be_shown_at_seattle_international_film_festival_2012">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/april/thames_delta_exhibition_in_southend">
         Thames Delta Exhibition in Southend
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        25 April 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  3:00
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          The Thames Delta Exhibition is a very important document to the profound effect that a small area has had on the World wide musical landscape. Many artists have submitted work to help illustrate this most dynamic of relationships.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          A selection of Dean's photographs of Southend bands are on show at
          <a href="http://www.southendmuseums.co.uk/">
           the Beecroft Art Gallery
          </a>
          which runs from 7th April-16th June.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wH1-vDBmek0/T5fHfLij2MI/AAAAAAAAAMc/dFZV_cUNNIo/s1600/Horr+nme2-049.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-wH1-vDBmek0/T5fHfLij2MI/AAAAAAAAAMc/dFZV_cUNNIo/s400/Horr+nme2-049.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          As you may already know
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean Chalkley
          </a>
          hails from Southend and has a strong affinity with the area. The music scene in Southend, centred around Junk Club circa 2006 became the focus of Dean's photographic collection "Southend's Underground". During this period Dean shot many up-and-coming bands from the area including
          <a href="http://www.thehorrors.co.uk/">
           The Horrors
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/These_New_Puritans">
           These New Puritans
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.myspace.com/iamtheoreticalgirl">
           Theoretical Girl
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.neilschildren.co.uk/">
           Neil's Children
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ipso_facto">
           Ipso Facto
          </a>
          and more.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Split over two locations, The
          <a href="http://www.focalpoint.org.uk/exhibitions/current/39/">
           Thames Delta
          </a>
          Exhibition celebrates the rich and varied musical heritage of Southend-on-Sea, Canvey Island and Basildon from the late 1940's to the present day. Naturally, Dean was approached by the organisers and submitted an array of images of the musical talent from this small corner of Essex.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Part one of the Exhibition is at
          <a href="http://www.focalpoint.org.uk/exhibitions/current/">
           The Focal Point Gallery
          </a>
          and features works by contemporary artists including Ross Birrall, Matt Do and Scott King and runs from 16th April-30th June.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Part two, at
          <a href="http://www.southendmuseums.co.uk/whats_on/event/Thames-Delta">
           The Beecroft Art Galley
          </a>
          is an exhibition of ephemera and archive material relating to the rich musical history of the area. This is where Dean's images are located. Part two of The Thames Delta Exhibition at the Beecroft Galleryruns from 7th April-16th June.
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/april/thames_delta_exhibition_in_southend#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/april/thames_delta_exhibition_in_southend">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/march/young_souls_to_be_shown_at_southend_film_festival">
         Young Souls to be shown at Southend Film Festival
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        30 March 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  4:25
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Almost Grown Soul Club has linked up with the Southend~on~Sea Film Festival to present the 'Almost Grown Cellar Cinema Club'
          <br/>
          <br/>
          12th May 2012 - 3PM-8PM - ENTRANCE: FREE
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-AyyOy-xqplU/T5fADb0jkRI/AAAAAAAAAMQ/h7Nkt_aP3E4/s640/YoungSoulsSouthendPoster+2.jpg"/>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Taking place in the basement of the historic Royal Hotel,
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean Chalkley
          </a>
          's short film YOUNG SOULS will be shown on the hour every hour from 4PM-8PM in between sessions by The Black Cat DJ collective, who will spin the best in Northern Soul, Rhythm &amp; Blues and Ska to keep the essential club atmosphere Uptight and Outta Sight + a few surprises thrown in for good measure.
          <br/>
          Later that night the club will take over the entire hotel for an all night club session.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Almost Grown Cellar Cinema
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.blogger.com/goog_1633304459">
           The Royal Hotel
          </a>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.blogger.com/goog_1633304459">
           1 High St.
          </a>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.blogger.com/goog_1633304459">
           Southend~on~Sea
          </a>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.blogger.com/goog_1633304459">
           Essex
          </a>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://maps.google.co.uk/maps/place?q=southend+royal+hotel&amp;hl=en&amp;cid=7770594747110086664">
           SS11 JE
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Watch this space for more details of whats in store! :)
         </span>
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/march/the_new_faces_a_short_film_on_showstudiocom">
         The New Faces: A Short Film on SHOWstudio.com
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        09 March 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  4:35
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: large;">
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           Last night was the screening of
          </span>
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/" style="font-family: inherit;">
           Dean Chalkley'
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           s "
          </span>
          <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/The-New-Faces-A-Short-Film/390678914281673" style="font-family: inherit;">
           The New Faces: A Short Film
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           " at
          </span>
          <a href="http://www.wearetbc.com/" style="font-family: inherit;">
           The Book Club
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           , London.
          </span>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           For such a lively and well attended event the packed out basement of
          </span>
          <a href="http://www.wearetbc.com/" style="font-family: inherit;">
           The Book Club
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           was silent through out the 20min long film piece which delves into minds of three young British Mods captured in the
          </span>
          enthrallment
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           of a subculture. In the film we are privy to their refreshingly honest, personal and polarised views, rooted in the ideology of a Modernist culture. The film forms a hypnotic visual experience as well as being an incisive and engaging contemporary document. Its also a pin point in a perennial subculture that began in the 1960s and has evolved and lives on in this modern age. It was received last night with rapturous applause. It was a great night of people dancing and enjoying the passionately selected tunes by the film's subjects.
          </span>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           The film went live on
          </span>
          <a href="http://showstudio.com/" style="font-family: inherit;">
           SHOWstudio
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           .com today. Click
          </span>
          <a href="http://showstudio.com/project/the_new_faces" style="font-family: inherit;">
           Here
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           to see it!
          </span>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://showstudio.com/project/the_new_faces" style="font-family: inherit;">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bGD0luqFNuY/T1o7lVNSlEI/AAAAAAAAALw/0lxNbO0CTJU/s640/Screen+shot+2012-03-09+at+15.36.10.png"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.showstudio.com/" style="font-family: inherit;">
           SHOWstudio
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           is an award-winning fashion website, founded and directed by
          </span>
          <a href="http://nickknight.com/main.html" style="font-family: inherit;">
           Nick Knight.
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           It has consistently pushed the boundaries of communicating fashion and culture online.
          </span>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           "I'm really thrilled that the film is now screening on
          </span>
          <a href="http://showstudio.com/" style="font-family: inherit;">
           SHOWstudio.com
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           . The site is an institution dedicated to forward-thinking and challenging new work." -
          </span>
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/" style="font-family: inherit;">
           Dean Chalkley
          </a>
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           (2012).
          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>

         Dean Chalkley: Special Guest Speaker at "Listen to This"
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        21 February 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  4:44
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Following on from
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean
          </a>
          's stint at
          <a href="http://www.whitewallspace.co.uk/">
           The White Wall Space Gallery
          </a>
          , Leigh~on~Sea with his Music portraits retrospective "
          <a href="http://www.whitewallspace.co.uk/dean_chalkley.html">
           LOOK HEAR
          </a>
          " (on until 29th Feb).
          <br/>
          <br/>

          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean
          </a>
          has been invited along to
          <a href="http://www.metalculture.com/">
           Metal
          </a>
          's Popular music and culture festival "
          <a href="http://www.metalculture.com/southend-on-sea/listen-to-this.html">

          </a>

           Dean
          </a>
          will be discussing the subculture in which he immersed himself whilst growing up in Southend and how they have remained at the core of his inspiration.

          <a href="http://listentothisfebruary24-eorg.eventbrite.com/">
           here
          </a>
          to purchase tickets for the event which will be held on Friday 20 April 2012 7.30pm  10pm at Chalkwell Hall, Southend on Sea. or call 01702 470700

        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        15 February 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  4:48
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Ex5tuGnlnSc/TzuSIys1pvI/AAAAAAAAALA/9uIHiQzyUDo/s1600/DC_CA_smith_poster_01.jpg" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Ex5tuGnlnSc/TzuSIys1pvI/AAAAAAAAALA/9uIHiQzyUDo/s640/DC_CA_smith_poster_01.jpg" width="440"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          LOOK.HEAR
         </span>
        </div>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Special Sunday Session: 19th February
         </span>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          11am-1pm
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Dean and renowned Photographer's Agent
          <a href="http://www.shootgroup.com/">
           Adele Rider
          </a>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          will be reviewing photographers portfolios at the
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <a href="http://www.whitewallspace.co.uk/">
           White Wall Space Gallery
          </a>
          Places are subject to availability so please apply by friday 17th February for your slot by mailing info@whitewallspace.co.uk... The gallery will reply with your allocated time.
         </span>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          2pm
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/february/young_souls_film_at_cinequest_film_festival">
         Young Souls Film at Cinequest Film Festival
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        08 February 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  5:02
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          The Festival is attended by 80,000 and although over 2,000 films are submitted each year only 188 films are shown and so we feel very honored that
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean Chalkley
          </a>
          's
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           YOUNG SOULS
          </a>
          is among the final selection.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3G8QUE_BW58/TzKNrVtYkOI/AAAAAAAAAK4/9LVrDda25F4/s1600/YoungSoulsPoster2Whiteweb.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3G8QUE_BW58/TzKNrVtYkOI/AAAAAAAAAK4/9LVrDda25F4/s640/YoungSoulsPoster2Whiteweb.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.cinequest.org/event_view.php?eid=1677">
           Cinequest
          </a>
          is an annual independent film festival held in San Jose, California.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          2012 is Cinequest's 22nd year and takes place from February 28th until March 11th.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.cinequest.org/event_view.php?eid=1677">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ubAajDrWRI8/TzKGnHH5EaI/AAAAAAAAAKs/rMKvKc-M66o/s1600/Cinequest+Programe.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           YOUNG SOULS
          </a>
          will be shown in the Shorts Program under "Give-and-Take" alongside 5 others.
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Here is what the organisers had to say about the selections:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          "What sacrifices must one make?
          <br/>
          No matter how it's defined, most people enjoy successes, but what we rarely reflect upon are the losses we suffer. Give-and-Take highlights the good and the bad of our endeavors. This program questions how much effort we are willing to put fourth to achieve our desire and to what lengths we are willing to go. But ultimately, these creative and inspiring shorts help us identify what we really value as individuals and determine for which ambitions we are willing to fight."
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           Young Souls
          </a>
          will be shown on the following dates:
          <br/>
          01/03/12 at 2:15 pm
          <br/>
          06/03/12 at 4:30 pm
          <br/>
          08/03/12 at 07:00pm
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Click
          <a href="http://www.cinequest.org/event_view.php?eid=1677">
           here
          </a>
          to buy tickets to
          <a href="http://www.cinequest.org/event_view.php?eid=1677">
           "Give-and-Take"
          </a>
          Shorts Program 3 where
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           YOUNG SOULS
          </a>
          will be screened.
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2012/february/young_souls_film_at_cinequest_film_festival#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2012/february/young_souls_film_at_cinequest_film_festival">
         </fb:comments-count>

        </a>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/february/lookhear_now_open">
         Look.Hear - Now Open
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        06 February 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  5:10
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          After a fantastic opening night on Friday 3rd Feb the White Wall Space gallery has now opened its doors to the public for
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/html/home.htm">
           Dean Chalkley
          </a>
          s new Exhibition
          <a href="http://deanchalkley.blogspot.com/2012/01/look-hear-new-exhibition.html">
           LOOK HEAR
          </a>
          .
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-211QGMlsNz8/Ty_LsaSJKeI/AAAAAAAAAKU/FJ1M8tZQh3g/s1600/423486_366154133397468_255145837831632_1500333_1796830037_n.jpeg">

          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The Opening party of
          <a href="http://deanchalkley.blogspot.com/2012/01/look-hear-new-exhibition.html">
           LOOK HEAR
          </a>
          was a great success, packed with people enjoying the work and the after show with its
          <a href="http://www.newstreetadventure.co.uk/">
           Band
          </a>
          and music all added up to a great happening.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Im keen to get down to the
          <a href="http://www.whitewallspace.co.uk/gallery.html">
           White WallSpace Gallery
          </a>
          and meet people who come to see
          <a href="http://deanchalkley.blogspot.com/2012/01/look-hear-new-exhibition.html">
           LOOK HEAR
          </a>
          . So Ill hopefully be there every Sunday. There will also be some spontaneous live music added to the mix. So keep an eye out on the B
          <a href="http://deanchalkley.blogspot.com/">
           log
          </a>
          and the
          <a href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/132952516774309/">
           Facebook
          </a>
          for the latest news!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          So thanks to all who came down, and all those who made the event such a high point - the DJs, the band 
          <a href="http://www.myspace.com/newstreetadventure">
           New StreetAdventure
          </a>
          , all those that worked at the gallery, my assistant, just to mention a few. 
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean Chalkley
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-U7ctliC3nas/Ty_L8HdHZDI/AAAAAAAAAKc/-Ts8C9-iwJY/s1600/409035_366154886730726_255145837831632_1500339_32521718_n.jpeg">

          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          So far the event has had plenty of radio coverage. The entire after show over at The Ship was broadcast live on
          <a href="http://radio.novalujon.com/03-02-12-dean-chalkley-look-hear/">
           Radio Nova Lujon
          </a>
          by Dave "Jazz DJ" Dawson, Click
          <a href="http://radio.novalujon.com/03-02-12-dean-chalkley-look-hear/">
           here
          </a>
          for an excerpt. Early on in the night on day
          <a href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/local/essex/hi/tv_and_radio/newsid_8177000/8177783.stm">

          <a href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/local/essex/hi/tv_and_radio/newsid_8177000/8177783.stm">

        <a href="2012/january/dean_chalkleys_bookshelf_on_its_nice_that">
         Dean Chalkley's Bookshelf on It's Nice That
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        30 January 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  5:27
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Every week
          <a href="http://www.itsnicethat.com/articles/bookshelf-dean-chalkley">
           It's Nice That
          </a>
          invite someone working from the creative industries to share with the world their most favourite five books.
         </span>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-JKZpwweb9SU/TybhCk7JlWI/AAAAAAAAAKE/eAN-Cz_r-t0/s1600/Screen+shot+2012-01-30+at+18.26.35.png">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-JKZpwweb9SU/TybhCk7JlWI/AAAAAAAAAKE/eAN-Cz_r-t0/s640/Screen+shot+2012-01-30+at+18.26.35.png"/>
         </a>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean
          </a>
          was asked to submit which books he draws inspiration from and why, along with a picture of the bookshelf in which they are housed.
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Among Dean's selection was
          <a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/mods">
           'Mods!' by Richard Barnes
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/electric-kool-aid-acid-test">
           'The Electric Kool-Aid Acid Test' by Tom Wolfe
          </a>
          and more... Click
          <a href="http://www.itsnicethat.com/articles/bookshelf-dean-chalkley">
           here
          </a>
          to read why!
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>

        </a>

       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/january/lookhear_new_exhibition">
         Look.Hear - New Exhibition
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        17 January 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  5:40
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean Chalkley's
          </a>
          brand new exhibition LOOK HEAR will be taking place at the
          <a href="http://www.whitewallspace.co.uk/gallery.html">
           White Wallspace Gallery
          </a>
          in Leigh-on-Sea.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-z-OyDwQUGBc/TxWLwwy1fnI/AAAAAAAAAJ8/UkQcEckfHI8/s1600/lookhear_invite.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-z-OyDwQUGBc/TxWLwwy1fnI/AAAAAAAAAJ8/UkQcEckfHI8/s640/lookhear_invite.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Opening night is on Friday 3rd February 2012 and will kick off at the Gallery where Dean will be showing a collection of some of his most iconic music photography. Featuring the likes of
          <a href="http://www.whitestripes.com/">
           The White Stripes
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.oasisinet.com/">
           Oasis
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.paulweller.com/">
           Paul Weller
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.kasabian.co.uk/gb/home/">
           Kasabian
          </a>
          and more with images what span a decade.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Following on from the gallery the party will move across the way to The Ship public house where attendants will be treated to the sounds of the soulful six piece
          <a href="http://www.newstreetadventure.co.uk/">
           New Street Adventure
          </a>
          + DJ's, dancing... ...What more do you expect from a Chalkley 'do'!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          LOOK HEAR will be open to the public from Saturday 4th February til 20th February 2012!
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2012/january/the_maccabees_nme">
         The Maccabees - NME
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        09 January 12
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  5:44
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          This week's issue of NME features Dean Chalkley's shoot of
         </span>
         <a href="http://www.themaccabees.co.uk/" style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          The Maccabees
         </a>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          as their cover and inside feature.
         </span>
         <a href="http://www.themaccabees.co.uk/" style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          The Maccabees
         </a>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          are on the cusp of releasing their new, eagerly anticipated third album
         </span>
         <a href="http://www.themaccabees.co.uk/#music/given-to-the-wild" style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          'Given to the Wild'
         </a>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          .
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Last week
          <a href="http://www.nme.com/news/various-artists/61283">
           The Maccabees
          </a>
          attended the NME Music Photography Awards where Dean accepted the '
          <a href="http://www.nme.com/news/various-artists/61283">
           Outstanding Contribution to Music Photography Award'
          </a>
          . The busy event was also attended by
          <a href="http://www.myignorantyouth.com/">
           Kate Nash
          </a>
          and comedian

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/december/dean_chalkleys_playlist_on_rose_blakes_studio_music">
         Dean Chalkley's Playlist on Rose Blake's Studio Music
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        13 December 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:04
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Dean was approached a few months back and asked if hed like to take part in the newly launched
          <a href="http://www.studiomusic.fm/index.html">
           Studio Music
          </a>
          .
          <br/>
          <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-pcNFgcv-o_k/TucouM7VOKI/AAAAAAAAAJY/zuCPQv19TPw/s1600/Screen+shot+2011-12-13+at+10.27.25.png">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-pcNFgcv-o_k/TucouM7VOKI/AAAAAAAAAJY/zuCPQv19TPw/s640/Screen+shot+2011-12-13+at+10.27.25.png"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Illustrator
          <a href="http://www.rose-blake.co.uk/">
           Rose Blake
          </a>
          has been asking creatives to select 10 inspirational/favorite songs that they listen to whilst working with a brief explanation as to why they like them.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The results are then published in the form of playlist on
          <a href="http://studiomusic.fm/">
           studiomusic.fm
          </a>
          The playlists are free to listen to and updated weekly.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Deans selection went live this week and can be found
          <a href="http://www.studiomusic.fm/index.html">
           here
          </a>
          alongside other contributors such as
          <a href="http://www.nodaysoff.com/">
           No Days Off
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.itsnicethat.com/">
           Its Nice That
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.stellamccartney.com/default/">
           Stella McCartney
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.emininternational.com/">
           Tracy Emin
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.legun.co.uk/">
           Le Gun
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="http://www.misterrob.co.uk/">
           Rob Ryan
          </a>
          and
          <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peter_Blake_(artist)">
           Peter Blake
          </a>
          to name but a few.
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2011/december/dean_chalkleys_playlist_on_rose_blakes_studio_music#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2011/december/dean_chalkleys_playlist_on_rose_blakes_studio_music">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

        <a href="2011/december/young_souls_to_be_shown_at_london_short_film_festival">
         Young Souls to be shown at London Short Film Festival
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        09 December 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:09
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.roxybarandscreen.com/info.php" style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kA_Ji2JZpME/TuIYAtHYOcI/AAAAAAAAAJQ/sxLRWoN8vfs/s640/YoungSoulsPoster2.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          We've had to keep this under our hat for a few weeks so Im very proud to finally be able to revieal that
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/">
           Dean Chalkley
          </a>
          s short film
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           Young Souls
          </a>
          has been selected to be shown at the 9th
          <a href="http://2011.shortfilms.org.uk/about/">
           London Short Film Festival!
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The Festival will take place between the 6th and 15th of January 2012 at the
          <a href="http://www.roxybarandscreen.com/info.php">
           Roxy Bar &amp; Screen
          </a>
          in Borough, London and will screen 24 Programmes of New British Shorts, showcasing nearly 300 new short films from British Filmmakers.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Young Souls will be screened as part of the New Shorts 16: Music &amp; Video Program, on Thursday 12th January 2012.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          To see it for yourself and be treated to a total of 152 mins (+interval) of the best british short films chosen by LSFF based on their marriage of sound and image, click
          <a href="http://www.tickettailor.com/checkout/view-event/id/2288/chk/070c">
           here
          </a>
          for tickets:

          http://www.tickettailor.com/checkout/view-event/id/2288/chk/070c
         </a>

          For more about the Listings on the 12/02/12 click
          <a href="http://www.roxybarandscreen.com/listings.php?event=1864">
           here
          </a>
          :

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/november/dean_chalkley_wins_nmes_outstanding_contribution_to_music_photography_award">
         Dean Chalkley wins NME's "Outstanding Contribution To Music Photography" Award.
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        16 November 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:50
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          We are extremely pleased to announce that NME Magazine has named Dean Chalkley the winner of their Outstanding Contribution To Music Photography Award.
         </span>
         <br/>
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-EH3oYUbK544/TsOLJSv2IoI/AAAAAAAAAIo/DGp0s6il5cU/s1600/NMEPhotoAwardsWinner.jpg">
          <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-EH3oYUbK544/TsOLJSv2IoI/AAAAAAAAAIo/DGp0s6il5cU/s640/NMEPhotoAwardsWinner.jpg"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          In their issue dated 05.11.2011 (which featured Deans cover shot of the Arctic Monkeys in Fort Lauderdale) NME said:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          From shooting Arctic Monkeys for our Radar section to capturing Pete Doherty being set on fire  and plenty more besides - Dean Chalkley has been responsible for some of the most iconic music photography for the past 10 years.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Further celebrating this in their 12.11.11 issue, NME published 4 posters in it's centre pages taken from the vast Chalkley back-catalogue of work with the NME. This included a picture of the late Amy Winehouse, Ian Brown, the formentioned Pete Doherty picture as well as the winner of The Picture Editor's Portrait of the year award, which features Noel Gallagher.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-gMmLfxU4dSs/TsOVpE3Ju3I/AAAAAAAAAIw/a0w1hI75Ztg/s1600/NME+AWARD.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-gMmLfxU4dSs/TsOVpE3Ju3I/AAAAAAAAAIw/a0w1hI75Ztg/s1600/NME+AWARD.jpg"/>
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2011/november/dean_chalkley_wins_nmes_outstanding_contribution_to_music_photography_award#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2011/november/dean_chalkley_wins_nmes_outstanding_contribution_to_music_photography_award">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/november/robert_2_in_reading_museums_permanent_collection">
         Robert #2 in Reading Museum's permanent collection.
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        16 November 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:26
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-left: 36.0pt;">
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          After having exhibited his collection "
          <a href="http://www.creativereview.co.uk/cr-blog/2010/march/exhibition-the-new-faces">
           The New Faces
          </a>
          " at
          <a href="http://www.readingmuseum.org.uk/">
           Reading Museum
          </a>
          for their "Reading Steady Go! Exhibition" which ran from 6th April 2011 until 9th October 2011, Dean Chalkley offered "Robert #2" as a gift to the Museum.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DegYz5bS2Sg/T6AA-9gndWI/AAAAAAAAAMo/nz5hYCf36v8/s1600/DSCF0314.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-DegYz5bS2Sg/T6AA-9gndWI/AAAAAAAAAMo/nz5hYCf36v8/s640/DSCF0314.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          This offer to donate the picture featuring the Reading-born subject "Robert Grindrod" was brought forward to the Reading Museum's acquistion's group.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          We've recieved the wonderful news that the committee was unanimous in accepting this offer to add this picture to the Museum's fine art collection.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          We are told that the museum's curators are concidering hanging "Robert #2" next to Gilbert Spencer's portrait "
          <a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/arts/yourpaintings/paintings/reading-boy-41673">
           Reading Boy
          </a>
          " of 1923; Wonderful news!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          We'll keep you posted with more news on this soon, so watch this space...
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2011/november/robert_2_in_reading_museums_permanent_collection#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2011/november/robert_2_in_reading_museums_permanent_collection">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/november/dazed_and_confused_making_it_up_as_we_go_along">
         Dazed and Confused: Making It Up As We Go Along
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        08 November 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 10:56
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-oFDDn6j5Jq4/TrlfLxJ9LTI/AAAAAAAAAIY/qecsOUV6hNk/s1600/angus+f+1+1.jpg">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-oFDDn6j5Jq4/TrlfLxJ9LTI/AAAAAAAAAIY/qecsOUV6hNk/s320/angus+f+1+1.jpg"/>
         </a>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Today we received a copy of Dazed and Confused: 'Making It Up As We Go Along'.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          It is a book plotting the visual history of the Magazine. '
          <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dazed_%26_Confused_(magazine)">
           Dazed
          </a>
          ' has been the 'enfant terible' of the Magazine world, challenging convention and breaking the rules. Many great Photographers, Artists, Stylist, etc. have worked on projects for the publication.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The main body of the book is delivered through photography producing an very stimulating and pleasurable read. Dean shot many projects for Dazed in the past, included in 'Making It Up As We Go Along' are Ice -T and George Clinton, as well as a special artist series with the late
          <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Angus_Fairhurst">
           Angus Fairhurst
          </a>
          (the images of which are included here).
         </span>
         <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2011/november/dazed_and_confused_making_it_up_as_we_go_along#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2011/november/dazed_and_confused_making_it_up_as_we_go_along">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/november/arctic_monkeys_nme">
         Arctic Monkeys - NME
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        03 November 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 11:00
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZvnyeZgggdg/TrKwgJjBY-I/AAAAAAAAAIA/fu0HovkP208/s1600/am.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="456" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZvnyeZgggdg/TrKwgJjBY-I/AAAAAAAAAIA/fu0HovkP208/s640/am.jpg" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         <br/>
        </p>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mXeW3S7lLOA/TrKw2q38dWI/AAAAAAAAAII/tBrCemI2MHQ/s1600/am1.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="472" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-mXeW3S7lLOA/TrKw2q38dWI/AAAAAAAAAII/tBrCemI2MHQ/s640/am1.jpg" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          The
         </span>
         <a href="http://arcticmonkeys.com/" style="font-family: inherit; font-size: x-large;">
          Arctic Monkeys
         </a>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          have been on the road in the States; NME flew Dean and journalist
         </span>
         <a href="http://twitter.com/#!/w1lko" style="font-family: inherit; font-size: x-large;">
          Matt Wilkinson
         </a>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          out to Fort Lauderdale to catch up with the band on their travels. What ensued was a story with clear parallels to the rock flick 'Almost Famous'... The usually sunny state of Florida was hit by unexpected thunderstorms high winds and torrential showers but this didn't deter your intrepid photographer and Journalist Dodging Hobo's, hanging out in trailer parks and going to an insane Mansion all night party. Pick up a copy of the NME and read all about the crazy trip with insights to the band, the gig, and the very odd goings on in the "Sunshine State".
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2011/november/arctic_monkeys_nme#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2011/november/arctic_monkeys_nme">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/october/creative_review_the_photography_annual_2011_out_now">
         Creative Review the Photography Annual 2011 OUT NOW
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        27 October 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 11:04
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7vAQ7-6kOmw/TqlN-0uFkZI/AAAAAAAAAH4/ovZwq6cqTPs/s1600/cr.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-7vAQ7-6kOmw/TqlN-0uFkZI/AAAAAAAAAH4/ovZwq6cqTPs/s1600/cr.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </div>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          The Creative Review Photography Annual launch Party was a blast!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Last night the Aubin Gallery in London's East End was packed with the good and great of the design world, all there to celebrate the release of this special edition of the Creative Review Magazine.
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Dean, as mentioned in the blog yesterday has in total 3 things in the publication all were projected during the event.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          To see more of the publication and the Magazines Launch party click
          <a href="http://www.creativereview.co.uk/cr-blog/2011/october/cr-photography-annual-launch">
           here
          </a>
          ....oh and who is that smartly dressed chap in the second picture?
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>

         </fb:comments-count>

        </a>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/october/photography_annual_launch_night">
         Photography Annual Launch Night
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        26 October 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 11:07
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VCpukbBY0nU/TqfV_KzP4ZI/AAAAAAAAAHw/Z5YnLdJ0OJU/s1600/PA+2011+-+Selected+Logo.jpg">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VCpukbBY0nU/TqfV_KzP4ZI/AAAAAAAAAHw/Z5YnLdJ0OJU/s320/PA+2011+-+Selected+Logo.jpg"/>
         </a>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          The Annual aims to be the definitive collection of the best commercial photographic work during the year. Work included this year is not restricted to stills photography as a moving image element is also present. Dean has 3 pieces of work selected to appear in this years collection. A single image photographic entry, secondly a campaign for the agency Figtree 'Everything Everywhere' (you can see the making of the campaign
          <a href="http://www.figtreenetwork.com/work/?client=Everything+Everywhere">
           here
          </a>
          ), and the third being the film '
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           Young Souls
          </a>
          '. Creative Review is a publication that Dean loves, it's consistent reflection of the zeitgeist of contemporary visual design has inspired Dean for so many years to be included in 'The Annual', is a great Honor and one which Dean is thrilled about.
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2011/october/photography_annual_launch_night#comments">

         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
