       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/september/rip_david_honeyboy_edwards">
         R.I.P. David "Honeyboy" Edwards
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        16 September 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  5:40
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-r3omhPLFhmc/TnNadrEie-I/AAAAAAAAAGc/GUTnzX9JXdg/s1600/dhw020web.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-r3omhPLFhmc/TnNadrEie-I/AAAAAAAAAGc/GUTnzX9JXdg/s320/dhw020web.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          deanchalkley/camerpress
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Original Blues Legend David "Honeyboy" Edwards sadly passed away on the 29th August 2011. The Mississippi born Bluesman was born in 1915 and carried on playing as many as 100 shows a year right up until 2008. Even once this intensive touring period was over he still undertook performances across the globe until July 2011 when declining health forced retirement from public performance.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          "Honeyboy" won 2 Grammy's one in 2008 for his album "Last of the Great Mississippi Delta Bluesmen : Live in Dallas" and a lifetime achievement award in 2010.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          As the title of the album states he was one of the greats! Through his long career he played with all the Godfathers of the Blues scene including Robert Johnson, Charley Patton, Johnny Shines, Muddy Waters and Howlin Wolf.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Dean took this photograph whilst David "Honeyboy" Edwards at the The Luminaire, Kilburn, London on 25th September 2009. By all accounts it was a brilliant gig and the warm personality, charm and pure musical talent of the 'Man' enveloped the enthralled audience.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          To read more and get into the music of this Legendary Delta Bluesman go to
          <a href="http://davidhoneyboyedwards.com/">
           David "Honeyboy" Edwards
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2011/september/rip_david_honeyboy_edwards#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2011/september/rip_david_honeyboy_edwards">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

          <br/>
          <br/>
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-00zcatNMwQk/TmTeoLw-j4I/AAAAAAAAAGQ/aw9k4BvLxqk/s640/mag_blog+15738h.jpg"/>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          In the accompanying interview with Emma John, Cumberbatch talks about immersing himself in the historical context and cultures surrounding the roles he plays as well as punching
          <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tom_Hardy">
           Tom Hardy
          </a>
          and adjusting to being single after 12 years.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/tv-and-radio/2011/sep/04/benedict-cumberbatch-ford-madox-ford">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-E_0xUPm91cA/TmTe32MGpLI/AAAAAAAAAGU/BtloH0TTdlg/s640/mag_blog+15739h.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          You can read the interview online
          <a href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/tv-and-radio/2011/sep/04/benedict-cumberbatch-ford-madox-ford">
           here!
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/august/young_souls_liberation">
         Young Souls - LIBERATION!
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        31 August 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  5:02
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-S8U-X-vc-Lo/Tl5RNnuS4tI/AAAAAAAAAFo/PlV4VSSUxIs/s1600/dean1.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-S8U-X-vc-Lo/Tl5RNnuS4tI/AAAAAAAAAFo/PlV4VSSUxIs/s640/dean1.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eC-PL57zpn4/Tl5Q9LorXjI/AAAAAAAAAFk/FVMeHArVzpQ/s1600/dean2.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eC-PL57zpn4/Tl5Q9LorXjI/AAAAAAAAAFk/FVMeHArVzpQ/s640/dean2.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-s2seI3BC8-0/Tl5Qwu2AcWI/AAAAAAAAAFg/K1t2fvJR1wQ/s1600/dean3.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-s2seI3BC8-0/Tl5Qwu2AcWI/AAAAAAAAAFg/K1t2fvJR1wQ/s640/dean3.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Stephanie Binet from Liberation came over the channel last month to London to do a piece about Mod Culture. After coming to the premiere of Deans new short film YOUNG SOULS, which took place at Bethnal Green Working Mens Club in London, she traveled to Reading for the Reading Steady Go festival. The festival; run by Reading Museum is a retrospective of the explosion of 1960s youth culture and its legacy today. Here Stephanie also encountered Deans exhibition The New Faces exhibition, which is centered around a group of young modernists.
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
          The results of Stephanies exploration can be seen here in Liberation!
         </span>
        </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/august/young_souls_exhibition_closes">
         Young Souls - Exhibition Closes
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        17 August 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  4:51
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <a href="http://www.bjp-online.com/IMG/735/187735/deanchalkleyamy.jpg?1311846438">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="448" src="http://www.bjp-online.com/IMG/735/187735/deanchalkleyamy.jpg?1311846438" width="640"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Dean Chalkley's photographic exhibition and short film was being shown at PYMCA's Youth Club Gallery from the 22nd June untill the 16th August!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The Exhibition has now been taken down however you can still see the short film online at 125 Magazine's website. Click
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           here
          </a>
          to see it!
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Young Souls has received rave reviews, but don't just take my word for it! Here are a few online reviews:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.creativereview.co.uk/cr-blog/2011/july/dean-chalkeys-young-souls-exhibiiton">
           Creative Review
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.bjp-online.com/british-journal-of-photography/news/2097518/souls-run-free">
           British Journal of Photography
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          and
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.itsnicethat.com/whats-on/young-souls">
           It's Nice That
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          "[The] film... ...is seriously good in terms of the cinematography, sound, aesthetics etc., and (perfectly captured in the still photos) the dancing is so damn cool it hurts."- Bryony Quin, "It's Nice That"
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>

        </a>
       </h2>

       </h3>
       <div class="content">

           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-4OzXVCv3wdM/TjhgS-Z8ExI/AAAAAAAAAFU/CLg6CrtjGuM/s640/New_Faces_Reading+email+crop.jpg"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          BBC Radio Berkshire celebrates the opening of Deans Touring Exhibition 'The New Faces'.
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-berkshire-14316012">
           click here
          </a>
          to go to the BBC website it has a great gallery with several images from the show. Dean also gave an interview to the BBC live on air on the day of the Exhibitions Private View.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The Private View and Special Club night at the Reading Museum was on the evening of Friday 29th July, a great evening that went from the museum to the 3B's Club with great DJ sets from Readings Club Rude and Londons Black Cat Dj's (of which Dean is one).
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The Exhibition officially opened to the Public on the 30th July and the show is on until the 4th September
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.readingmuseum.org.uk/events/details/208/">
           Click here
          </a>
          for details of the Reading Museum, the link includes opening times and details of the Museums location.
         </span>
        </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/july/young_souls_exhibition_at_youth_club_popup">
         Young Souls Exhibition at Youth Club Pop-up
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        22 July 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  3:52
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
        </p>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-IjCj-U3vroI/Tim-0aRSntI/AAAAAAAAAFI/fMVA3iWmdJo/s1600/183838_204972192884918_137601766288628_510572_6584254_n.jpg">
          <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-IjCj-U3vroI/Tim-0aRSntI/AAAAAAAAAFI/fMVA3iWmdJo/s320/183838_204972192884918_137601766288628_510572_6584254_n.jpg"/>
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          james lange pymca
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Youth Club one of Londons newest and most happening Galleries hosted the Private View for Deans New Exhibition. The Gallery in Kingly Court (off Carnaby Street) London had a great turn out and was visited by lots of people eager to catch a first glimpse of the show.
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <a href="http://www.facebook.com/media/set/?set=a.204971646218306.52481.137601766288628">
           http://www.facebook.com/media/set/?set=a.204971646218306.52481.137601766288628
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Legendary Northern Soul DJ and Mr. 6T's / Kent Records Ady Croasdell was joined behind the decks by Donna Driscoll, Jo Wallace and Dean also popped a few choice 45's on too, the night was a very lively affair.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The show is now open to the public and runs until 4th August.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Saturdays inc 23rd July 1pm - 6pm
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Weekdays Mon - Fri 11am - 6pm
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The exhibition consists of 22 large prints some of which are exclusive to this show and there is also the opportunity to see the YOUNG SOULS film that is currently screening on
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/">
           www.125magazine.com
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The Galleries address is as follows for all enquires
          <br/>
          contact Youth Club direct:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="mailto:info@youthclublondon.com">
           info@youthclublondon.com
          </a>
          <br/>
          Telephone: +44(0) 20 7437 0391
          <br/>
          2.3 Kingly Court
          <br/>
          Carnaby Street
          <br/>
          London, W1B 5PW
          <br/>
          all images of the Private View Part shown here were taken by James Lange @ PYMCA
         </span>
        </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/july/young_souls_on_125magazinecom">
         Young Souls on 125magazine.com
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        15 July 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  3:34
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
         <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6MUxsmugdOw/TiB43kd4KsI/AAAAAAAAAFE/eB_LEVZMghI/s640/125+grab.jpg" style="font-family: inherit; font-size: x-large; float: left;"/>
        </div>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
          Last night Dean unveiled his new Short Film
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           YOUNG SOULS
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          There was an electric atmosphere in The Bethnal Green Working Men's Club last night as eminent Soul DJ's built up the excitement with their finely tuned record selections.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Then it was time!..
          <br/>
          <br/>
          YOUNG SOULS played at 9pm...
          <br/>
          <br/>
          As the film drew to a close the audiences cheers, whoops and applause confirmed that YOUNG SOULS is not only a beautifully engaging Art piece but an accessible thrilling and energizing expression made with integrity and passion.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          In total the film ran three times through the evening, each time to packed audiences. Between the screenings the DJ's kept the dance floors pulsing.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          As day broke and the night at Bethnal Green drew to a close YOUNG SOULS became available to view online at
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           www.125magazine.com
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Already the film has been viewed by an incredibly high number of viewers and amongst its plaudits..
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The Word Magazine Tweeted:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          "If you've ever totally lost yourself while dancing, this brilliant short film by @nitzerdc (dean chalkley) will bring it all back ..."
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Q Magazine Tweeted:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          "Get a Northern Soul fix with this smart new short film YOUNG SOULS from Dean Chalkley. You can smell the talc from here."
          <br/>
          <br/>
          So what are you waiting for get to:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/?p_id=300&amp;pg=488">
           www.125magazine.com
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2011/july/young_souls_on_125magazinecom#comments">

         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/june/f2_freelance_photographer_magazine_profile_on_dean_chalkley">
         F2 Freelance Photographer Magazine Profile on Dean Chalkley
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        06 June 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  3:24
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-KDrWcZPWH_w/TfDI0hu6MiI/AAAAAAAAAFA/dCaiEHqHjlc/s1600/Cover+June+REV.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-KDrWcZPWH_w/TfDI0hu6MiI/AAAAAAAAAFA/dCaiEHqHjlc/s640/Cover+June+REV.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Vol 5 No5 Issue of Freelance Photographer's special "Moving To London Graduate Guide" features 4 double page spreads dedicated to Dean in their F2 Profile section.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          "Top Music Photographer Dean Chalkley talks to David Land, about the changing nation of the industry, shooting HD video, and the importance of tangibility in achieving a cachet for your work."
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The interview touches upon Dean's soon-to-be-released short "Young Souls", his love of Northern Soul music, internships and much, much more.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          If you would like to get your hands on a copy you can buy it online by clicking
          <a href="http://www.f2freelancephotographer.com/backissues.html">
           HERE!
          </a>
          or alternatively F2 Magazine is also available from most WH Smiths High St. branches, The Photographers Gallery Book Shop, Harrods London and other specialist photographic outlets.
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/june/foo_fighters_nme">
         Foo Fighters - NME
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        01 June 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  3:16
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Dean Shot the Foo Fighters the day after he shot all of the winners at the 2011 NME Awards, where Dave Grohl won "Godlike Genius award". The photoshoot took place in and around The Vinyl Factory in London's Soho District. The Foos were in the UK to promote their new album
          <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wasting_Light">
           Wasting Light
          </a>
          and a new feature length documentary "Back and Forth" directed by James Moll, which Dean had the pleasure of seeing two nights previous to the shoot. Dean also got to see the band play at the end of the week at Wembley Arena too. So all in all a fun packed Foo Fighting Fantasia.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2fkh0kv_oK8/TeYrfWK31sI/AAAAAAAAAE0/tPJM-VfcHLQ/s1600/93NME11015140.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2fkh0kv_oK8/TeYrfWK31sI/AAAAAAAAAE0/tPJM-VfcHLQ/s640/93NME11015140.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The issue was released on 16.04.11
         </span>
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/april/young_souls_now_on_125_magazines_website">
         Young Souls now on 125 Magazine's website
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        07 April 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:56
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <br/>
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-PGSfMgNbzTs/TZ16IGx90HI/AAAAAAAAAEE/r5dxBUORiqI/s1600/Screen+shot+2011-04-07+at+09.46.54.png">
          <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-PGSfMgNbzTs/TZ16IGx90HI/AAAAAAAAAEE/r5dxBUORiqI/s320/Screen+shot+2011-04-07+at+09.46.54.png"/>
         </a>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Deans photographs of the YOUNG SOULS are now out in the Religion issue of 125MAGAZINE (Issue #17)
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The connection to Young Souls and the theme of the issue: Religion, Is the binding mantra of Northern Soul devotees: Keeping the Faith.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          For many years Dean has loved this music and culture so he felt it was time to make work around it.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          So here it is.
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/index.php?p_id=2">
           click here to find out more!
          </a>
          and
          <a href="http://www.125magazine.com/index.php?p_id=9">
           here
          </a>
          for stockists of the magazine.
         </span>
        </p>

        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">

       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:43
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          On the 4th of December 2010 SHAKE! at the boogaloo bar in Highgate was broadcast live on air on www.novalujon.com.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          This Audio Spectacular has now been cleaned up and is available to download in the shape of a podcast for FREE!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          http://radio.novalujon.com/04-12-10-shake/
          <br/>

          On this very special session at the Boogaloo, regular SHAKE! Deejays: Si Cheeba and Dean Chalkley were joined by the formidable Chap from Essex David JazzDJ Dawson. David has been an influential mover and shaker for many years with too many to mention deejay appearances at Clubs Glastonbury festivals etc. A great Deejay who, not only knows his music inside out but knows how to get the crowd up on their feet and dancing nonstop...not only that....David JazzDJ Dawson brought with him his broadcasting abilities. As the man behind cult internet radio station www.novalujon.com David streamed the atmosphere soaked tunes spun by Dean, Si and himself out to the world on the internet airwaves.

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/february/strip_now_on_vimeo">
         Strip now on Vimeo
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        11 February 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:04
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <img alt="" border="0" height="440" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-o_GPxFedvW0/TVUuyxySoRI/AAAAAAAAAD8/7fb5Oea3CEc/s640/Screen+shot+2011-02-11+at+12.41.20.png" width="640"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <span style="font-family: inherit;">
           <br/>
           Dean has just uploaded his short film 'Strip' onto
           <a href="http://vimeo.com/19791469">
            Vimeo
           </a>
           .
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Strip was Dean's first film and was made in the year 2000 and shot on super 8 film.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           With the support of the British Film Council, 'Strip' was successfully entered and screened at several short film festivals around the world and it won the Kinofilm 2000 Best Experimental Short Film award at the International Short Film Festival in Manchester.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Strip was written and produced by Dean Chalkley
           <br/>
           Music and Sound by Geir Jenssen
           <br/>
           and Edited by Suky Chiaranussati.
          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>

         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/january/soul_film_and_photography_project_club_scene_filming">
         Soul Film and Photography Project (club scene filming)
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        20 January 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:31
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          The filming side of the project will take place on 30th January in North London. This time we are planning to shoot some club scenes so we're looking for some more people to come along.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          All ages are welcome, so as long as you can dance to Northern and are interested in taking part please drop us an email to:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          info@lookslondon.com
          <br/>
          <br/>
          We have to receive an email from you - so please don't just join the Group -its important!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          If possible include a picture of yourself with what you might wear...even if its from your camera phone.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          There might be a limitation on numbers so please pass your details over as soon as you can!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The result will be a short film, not be a feature film and it doesnt set out to be the definitive story of Northern Soul youll be relieved to know, but it does aim to celebrate it.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Also I thought that it would be necessary to mention that this project has no outside funding, which means that Dean will be paying for the whole thing himself. Therefore what is being asked is for people to donate their time!
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Amanda Ashed
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Looks Agency
          <br/>
          020 8341 4477
          <br/>
          www.lookslondon.com
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/january/tony_christie_nows_the_time">
         Tony Christie - Now's the Time
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        07 January 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:41
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Tony Christie's new album is released today.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          'Now's the Time'; released on Acid Jazz Record label. All of the photos taken for the album where taken by Dean in various Soho haunts.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Tony has spent time rediscovering the soul side of his early career, and has encompassed this into the recording of an incredible album, which was produced by friend, fan and one time collaborator, Richard Barrett from The All Seeing Eye.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The album brings together the sound of Northern Soul, British Beat and filmic soundtracks. Tracks like Get Christie (a re-work of the iconic theme from Get Carter) features a collaboration with fellow Dee-Dar, Jarvis Cocker, other collaborations on the album come from Roisin Murphy amongst others.
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Available now in all good record shops, online, on iTunes
          <br/>
          &lt;
          <a href="http://itunes.apple.com/gb/album/nows-the-time/id413526601">
           http://itunes.apple.com/gb/album/nows-the-time/id413526601
          </a>
          &gt; and in our
          <br/>
          eBay Shop &lt;
          <a href="http://stores.ebay.co.uk/ACID-JAZZ-Shop">
           http://stores.ebay.co.uk/ACID-JAZZ-Shop
          </a>
          &gt;.
         </span>
         <br/>
         <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
          <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          </span>
         </div>
         <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
          <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TVAJ5ualoAI/AAAAAAAAADw/Kzt4cW_9DX4/s1600/51qaykb95ML.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
           <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
            <img alt="" border="0" height="320" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TVAJ5ualoAI/AAAAAAAAADw/Kzt4cW_9DX4/s320/51qaykb95ML.jpg" width="320"/>
           </span>
          </a>
         </div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          <br/>
          It's a great album! Don't take our word for it though... here's what The Guardian had to say about it:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          "Tony Christie considers this album to be "the real me"... ...Now's the Time! returns the 67-year-old crooner to his comfort zone of brassy lounge-pop and film soundtracks, and he sounds pleased to be there. And why not? His tenor, which forever hovers at the edge of quivering melodrama, was made for high-quality MOR like this. The best of a uniformly good bunch is 7 Hills, a deliciously sleazy country duet with Risn Murphy, but also worth hearing are the jazzy Too Much of the Sun, which casts him as an old rou melancholically looking back at his life, and Get Christie, a spoof of the Get Carter theme with lyrics by Jarvis Cocker ("If a job needs doing and needs doing right, who ya gonna trust? Get Christie!")."- Caroline Sullivan
          <br/>
          <br/>
          **** Tony Christie's 'Now's the Time' was given a 4/5 review ****
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2011/january/tony_christie_nows_the_time#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2011/january/tony_christie_nows_the_time">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/january/exciting_new_soul_photography_and_film_project">
         Exciting New Soul Photography and Film Project
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        07 January 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:27
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Dean is scouting for good, youthful Northern Soul dancers to feature in a short film and photographic project.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          It will be presented through the biannual culture and fashion magazine '125'.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          125 Magazine is a unique visual compendium of new ideas in photography, fashion, art and culture. Each issue is a tribute to creative freedom, showcasing breakthrough work by emerging and established creative's in a luxury 300 page edition.
          <br/>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          If you are a good northern soul dancer or know anyone who is; please send a video clip to show us your moves. We are looking for a mixture of young male and female soul enthusiasts who can dancewell to Northern Soul.
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Although we are interested in a variety of styles we are very keen to get people who can do the more acrobatic style of dancing.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          You must be available for the potential shooting days which are 16th Jan and the 30th Jan and will take place in a central London location.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          On the 16th of Jan a small group of dancers will be selected for the photographic element of the shoot and on the 30th of Jan a larger crowd will be needed for filming.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          If this sound like you then please send us a video to show us your moves. It will be an essental part of the selection process. If you could also send a photo or two this would be good too.
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Contact us with:
          <br/>
          <br/>
          your name
          <br/>
          video clip/s
          <br/>
          photo/s
          <br/>
          telephone number
          <br/>
          and e-mail address
          <br/>
          <br/>
          e-mailing this to the casting Director Amanda Ashed at
          <br/>
          <br/>
          info@lookslondon.com
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Once selected, successful applicants will be contacted by Amanda, who will explain all of the neccessary details about the photographic shoot and film.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Also, I felt it necessary to mention that this project has no outside funding, which means that Dean will be paying for the whole thing himself. Therefore what is being asked is for people to donate their time.
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>

        <a href="2011/january/exciting_new_soul_photography_and_film_project#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2011/january/exciting_new_soul_photography_and_film_project">

      <div class="post">
       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/january/the_new_faces_reading_steady_go_exhibition">
         The New Faces - Reading Steady Go! Exhibition
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        07 January 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at 12:22
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Dean's Exhibition the New Faces is being shown at Reading Museum and Town Hall as apart of a larger exhibition which explores Mod culture.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TSb2IsjbUfI/AAAAAAAAADU/ZwZobCi2x1s/s1600/RSG-logo-DATES-web.JPG">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TSb2IsjbUfI/AAAAAAAAADU/ZwZobCi2x1s/s400/RSG-logo-DATES-web.JPG"/>
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Reading Steady Go! Is an exploration into the explosion of youth culture in the 1960's and it's legacy in today's music and fashion. The museum aims to use the town's own experience of the impact of this particular youth subculture by displaying beloved artefacts from donators. The Museum is appealing for those who would like to lead their own material for the exhibition. So if you would like to get involved in enriching this display of this insightful exhibition please click here. or alternativly call the museaum on 0118 937 3400
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The exhibition will be running from the 9th April 2011 until 9th Oct 2011 as is sponsored by
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TSb6x9jVpvI/AAAAAAAAADY/7SUa8MdFgIs/s1600/Festival-Republic-logo.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TSb6x9jVpvI/AAAAAAAAADY/7SUa8MdFgIs/s1600/Festival-Republic-logo.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TSb60X0yxrI/AAAAAAAAADc/eXORzvHUJv8/s1600/PG-Colour-logo.jpg">
           <img alt="" border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TSb60X0yxrI/AAAAAAAAADc/eXORzvHUJv8/s1600/PG-Colour-logo.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <br/>
          <br/>
          To read more visit the
          <a href="http://www.readingmuseum.org.uk/events/details/95/">
           Reading Museum and Town Hall website
          </a>
          .
          <br/>
          <br/>
          To join the facebook page click
          <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Reading-Steady-Go-Life-Through-the-Eyes-of-a-1960s-Mod/150172888338727">
           here
          </a>
          .
         </span>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/january/serge_in_housegrey_magazine">
         Serge in Housegrey Magazine
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        05 January 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:12
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div id="text_2" style="color: white; font-family: Arial, Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; line-height: 15px; padding-bottom: 15px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 10px; padding-top: 0px; width: 500px; margin: 0px;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black; font-family: Times;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: small; line-height: normal;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TP4nTVPBekI/AAAAAAAAAC8/Jo7xxoGvsuQ/s1600/Screen+shot+2010-12-07+at+12.11.26.png" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="512" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TP4nTVPBekI/AAAAAAAAAC8/Jo7xxoGvsuQ/s640/Screen+shot+2010-12-07+at+12.11.26.png" width="640"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div id="text_2" style="color: white; font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; line-height: 15px; padding-bottom: 15px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 10px; padding-top: 0px; width: 500px; margin: 0px;">
         <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span style="color: black; font-size: large; line-height: normal;">
           Dean was asked to be a contributor to the online Magazine
          </span>
          <a href="http://housegrey./" style="font-size: x-large; line-height: normal;">
           Housegrey.
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div id="text_2" style="color: white; font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; line-height: 15px; padding-bottom: 15px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 10px; padding-top: 0px; width: 500px; margin: 0px;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: small; line-height: normal;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             The film was shot on super 8, written and directed by Dean,
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black; font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: large; line-height: normal;">
          a homage to the "
          <a href="http://www.britannica.com/EBchecked/topic/1100468/physical-culture">
           Physical Culturist
          </a>
          ".
         </span>
        </div>
        <div id="text_2" style="color: white; font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; line-height: 15px; padding-bottom: 15px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 10px; padding-top: 0px; width: 500px; margin: 0px;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: small; line-height: normal;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             The haunting soundtrack by icelandic contempory classical composer Johann Johannsson, is entitled "Odi et
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: small; line-height: normal;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             Amo".
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black; font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large; line-height: normal;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black; font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large; line-height: normal;">
           It recites Catullus' Ancient poem in Latin through the means of modern technology:
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="line-height: normal;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="line-height: normal;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
             I hate and I love. Wherefore would I do this, perhaps you ask?
             <br/>
             I do not know. But I feel that it happens and I am tortured.
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: small; line-height: normal;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: small; line-height: normal;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             Serge was edited by Spencer Doane.
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div id="text_2" style="color: white; font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; line-height: 15px; padding-bottom: 15px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 10px; padding-top: 0px; width: 500px; margin: 0px;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black; font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large; line-height: normal;">
           See it
           <a href="http://www.housegrey.com/">
            here
           </a>
           on Housegrey
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div id="text_2" style="color: white; font-size: 12px; font-style: normal; line-height: 15px; padding-bottom: 15px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 10px; padding-top: 0px; width: 500px; margin: 0px;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: black; font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: large; line-height: normal;">
          or
          <a href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/html/film_2_intro.htm">
           here
          </a>
          on Dean's own website.
         </span>
        </div>

          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">

Deejays: Si Cheeba and Dean Chalkley were joined by the formidable Chap from Essex David JazzDJ Dawson.David has been an influential mover and shaker for many years with too many to mention deejay appearances at Clubs Glastonbury festivals etc. A great Deejay who, not only knows his music inside out but knows how to get the crowd up on their feet and dancing nonstop...not only that....David JazzDJ Dawson brought with him his broadcasting abilities. As the
            </span>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2011/january/dale_ted_watkins_1">
         Dale Ted Watkins
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        05 January 11
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:30
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TP4rQS_eVBI/AAAAAAAAADA/S60M6_SMDXE/s1600/Screen+shot+2010-12-07+at+12.40.01.png" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="365" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TP4rQS_eVBI/AAAAAAAAADA/S60M6_SMDXE/s400/Screen+shot+2010-12-07+at+12.40.01.png" style="display: block; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;" width="400"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         <br/>
         <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: large;">
          Here is an interview with Dale Ted Watkins. Dale is an exceptional hairdresser who has worked on many shoots with Dean, the latest of which being Tony Christie's Press and Album shoots. He has spent nearly 30 years as a pioneer of mens hairdressing in the UK. Having trained and worked at Vidal Sassoon, Dale felt the mens market was where his passion lay and he has continued to take this passion through stints in London salons such as Refinery and Adams of London and his clients include Sasha Baron Cohen, Guy Ritchie and Jonny Owens.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Dales technical ability and knowledge of traditional barbering techniques puts him in constant demand as a session stylist.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Click
          <a href="http://myhairdressers.com/guests/dale-ted-watkins.html">
           here
          </a>
          to see the interview.
         </span>
        </p>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2010/december/paul_weller_find_the_torch_burn_the_plans">
         Paul Weller - Find The Torch, Burn The Plans
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        10 December 10
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  1:05
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-autospace: none;">
        </div>
        <p>
         <br/>
        </p>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Arial;">
          <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZjVUEHCiI/AAAAAAAAACs/8dDf0LLS2VI/s1600/602527437910.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="400" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZjVUEHCiI/AAAAAAAAACs/8dDf0LLS2VI/s400/602527437910.jpg" width="400"/>
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-pagination: none; text-autospace: none;">
         <span style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <p>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Arial;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Times;">
           <br/>
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             Paul Weller has just released a very special double DVD and CD of the acclaimed Julien Temple film 'Find The Torch, Burn The Plans' alongside a concert filmed at London's Royal Albert Hall.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             Deans picture features on the cover of the Single of the same name.
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Arial;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Times;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Arial;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Times;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             The DVD package comes complete in a deluxe hardback case with previously unseen photos of Wellers year and exclusive sleeve notes Paul Moody interviewing Weller - a must buy for any Paul Weller fan!The DVD is bolstered by the '7&amp;3 Is The Strikers Name' promo video directed by Lawrence Watson.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             In addition there is a CD featuring 12 songs from the Royal Albert Hall show plus six tracks from Wellers in concert at the BBC Theatre show - including collaborations with Richard Hawley and Lauren Pritchard.
             <br/>
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <div>
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">

            <br/>

            <br/>

            <br/>

            <br/>

        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        04 December 10
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:30
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <br/>
         <br/>
        </p>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZY9l6T6SI/AAAAAAAAACk/0zvYVcXVkGw/s1600/Shot_07_Tinchy_RGB.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
            <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZY9l6T6SI/AAAAAAAAACk/0zvYVcXVkGw/s640/Shot_07_Tinchy_RGB.jpg" width="478"/>
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <p>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           Third Strike was released on November 15, 2010 it's Tinchys third studio album and his second album with Island Records.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           The shoot for the album and singles was done in two parts.
          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           The first part of the shoot took place at Big Sky Studios London. Dean shot Tinchy in this environment to get the 'raw material' to project in the second part of the shoot. Part two of the project was epic, the studio shots were projected on to a huge abandoned
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
          secret location in London. T
         </span>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
          he projector was so big it had it's own lorry and i
         </span>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
          n the dead of that night Tinchy stood tall visable for miles.
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           Heres how the picture looked on the album...
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZZn79UuqI/AAAAAAAAACo/Bo7soejR-yw/s1600/1289550361_tinchy-stryder-third-strike-2010.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="400" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZZn79UuqI/AAAAAAAAACo/Bo7soejR-yw/s400/1289550361_tinchy-stryder-third-strike-2010.jpg" width="400"/>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2010/november/luellas_guide_to_english_style">
         Luella's Guide to English Style
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        29 November 10
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:44
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPPjRuYOnpI/AAAAAAAAAA4/4g2mdOE807U/s1600/Luella_main.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPPjRuYOnpI/AAAAAAAAAA4/4g2mdOE807U/s640/Luella_main.jpg" width="524"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Times;">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: small;">
             <br/>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           Luella Bartley has recently released a book titled Luellas Guide to English Style. Luella chose Deans picture of Dizzee Rascal to feature in the book.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           This charming book is a beautifully-bound, traditional, embossed hardback and is guide to the social style rituals of Britain.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           The former journalists study is a social, anthropological one supported by photographs, illustrations and occasional diagrams (which appear as numbered plates).
           <br/>
           <br/>
           The seriousness of the books exterior, along with the traditional layout, present a light hearted and humorous content which explores contemporary themes through chapters covering Tradition English Garb, fashion values according to class and the different Tribes of Britannia.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Deans picture (plate No. 33) supports Luellas analysis of Grime where she credits Grime artists such as Dizzee for salvaging working-class style form the chav, by injecting back into it a bit of humor and satire. The picture was taken from the front cover of Dizzee Rascals debut album Boy in Da Corner, which was shot by Dean.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           In all the book looks beautiful and is both enlightening to the uninitiated and affirming to the familiar. A really nice read.
          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2010/november/luellas_guide_to_english_style#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2010/november/luellas_guide_to_english_style">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2010/november/matthew_williamson_book">
         Matthew Williamson Book
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        29 November 10
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:27
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPPh49Q-ZdI/AAAAAAAAAA0/e-lZqsB70TQ/s1600/M_Williamson_main.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPPh49Q-ZdI/AAAAAAAAAA0/e-lZqsB70TQ/s640/M_Williamson_main.jpg" width="524"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div>
        </div>
        <div>
         <div class="MsoNormal">
          <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            British Fashion Designer Matthew Williamson is the subject of a new book by internationally renowned publishing house Rizzoli which was released on the 18th October 2010.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            The book is a definitive volume, exploring Matthews life, work and achievements. It is a wholly absorbing experience of riotous colour.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Deans contribution to the book is a picture of Matthew in his home. Matthew sits amongst his interesting bright and colourful study, its clear to see all his influences, including the Indian inspired colour pallet that permeates into his work for the likes of Pucci and his own eponymous label.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            The Book comprises of numerous photographs by the worlds top fashion photographers. Images of shows, collections, and even personal snapshots and sketches by Matthew himself are contained within its pages. Colin McDowell; the author of the book, chronicles Matthews career, from his debut collection, Electric Angels to his 10-year anniversary show giving a unique insight into the life of one of Britains most celebrated designers.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Dean was kindly invited along to the books launch on Tuesday 12th October at Somerset house. A concurrent exhibition is being held there until January 2011, featuring images from the book. Heres what Matthew Williamson said about the night:
            <br/>
            <br/>
            "This book feels like a new chapter in my life, it was so personal to me. It is amazing to be here with all my close friends.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Click
           </span>
           <a href="http://www.matthewwilliamson.com/home/promotion2/2010/09/matthew-williamson-book">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             here
            </span>
           </a>
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            to read more about the book.
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </div>

         </fb:comments-count>

        </a>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2010/november/kings_of_leon_in_london_for_uncut">
         Kings of Leon- in London for Uncut
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        29 November 10
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  6:29
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPO3D2eR9VI/AAAAAAAAAAw/EFAUFszutJ8/s1600/kol_uncut_main.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPO3D2eR9VI/AAAAAAAAAAw/EFAUFszutJ8/s640/kol_uncut_main.jpg" width="454"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
        </div>
        <p>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           The week following Deans trip to New York to shoot Kings of Leon for the NME, the Kings of Leon came to the UK. This time the session took place at the beautiful Connaught Hotel, for Uncut Magazine.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           The Magazine has run a six double-page spread on the Kings, with an interview by Jaan Uhelszki in which the Kings talk about their early songwriting days, recalling stories of a prophetic preachers from back home, as well as artistic differences in the band and of course the obligatory family bust-ups.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           The magazine, which came out this week, also features a review of the Kings of Leon album Come Around Sundown, which they have given 4/5 stars.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           To read more go to http://www.uncut.co.uk/news/uncut/news/14356
          </span>
         </span>

        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">

        </div>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZs1O5JsaI/AAAAAAAAACw/kA7ZxGn7bgY/s1600/PaulWellerNME.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZs1O5JsaI/AAAAAAAAACw/kA7ZxGn7bgY/s640/PaulWellerNME.jpg" width="524"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <p>
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           Deans picture of Paul Weller was chosen to be on the front cover of the NME this week.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Inside, Paul shares his thoughts on his musical past, his triumphant 2010 and confirms he has no plans to quit touring and recording music any time soon.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           He tells the music weekly: "If I can still stand up, I will be (touring), definitely. I don't think there's any end to it, until I drop dead."
           <br/>
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
         <br/>
         <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
          <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZusMKVIoI/AAAAAAAAAC0/_98clukQtmc/s1600/Screen+shot+2010-12-01+at+15.49.09.png" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
           <img alt="" border="0" height="452" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPZusMKVIoI/AAAAAAAAAC0/_98clukQtmc/s640/Screen+shot+2010-12-01+at+15.49.09.png" width="640"/>
          </a>
         </div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div>
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           Also in this issue is a free poster give away section to promote the new NME Collection at
           <a href="http://soniceditions.com/collection/nme">
            Sonic Editions
           </a>
           .
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Dean, along with
           <a href="http://www.andywillsher.com/">
            Andy Willsher
           </a>
           and
           <a href="http://www.tomoxley.com/">
            Tom Oxley
           </a>
           have submitted a selection of photographs of various iconic artists for the NME.
           <br/>

           The sonic editions are limited to 495 per image and come in a range of 3 print sizes, with various framing and mounting options and are available to buy online. Click

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2010/november/streetstyle_book_new_edition">
         Streetstyle Book New Edition!
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        25 November 10
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  3:47
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TO6DjteDsqI/AAAAAAAAAAU/FrRVX0RtC2k/s1600/set_up_club_PYMCA_main.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="265" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TO6DjteDsqI/AAAAAAAAAAU/FrRVX0RtC2k/s400/set_up_club_PYMCA_main.jpg" width="400"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          Streetstyle new edition book launch at The Book Club in conjunction with PYMCA
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            (Photographic Youth Movement Culture Archive)
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            PYMCA have unveiled a new edition of the seminal work by
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <a href="http://www.tedpolhemus.com/main_concept6%20467.html">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            <span lang="EN-US">
             <span lang="EN-US">
              Ted Polhemus
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </a>
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            , Streetstyle. Fashion icon
           </span>
          </span>
          <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chlo%C3%AB_Sevigny">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            <span lang="EN-US">
             <span lang="EN-US">
              Chloe Sevigny
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </a>
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            has been quoted by The New York Times as referring to Streetstyle as her Sartorial Bible.
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            First published by Thames and Hudson in 1994, the book was instantly successful and had a profound effect, describing and documenting how youth subcultures grew, manifested themselves and evolved.
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            As its title implies, it focuses on styles and trends that emanate from the street, having a trickle-up effect, eventually reaching high fashion status.
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            Deans pictures have been selected to feature in, not only the book but also in the exhibition.
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            The Private view of the exhibition/book launch and signing took place at the Book Club, London on 30th September. You can get your hands on a singed copy by Ted Polhemus from
           </span>
          </span>
          <a href="http://www.pymca.com/index.php?18066741369785505080.0000183227504077103110425112010163611">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            <span lang="EN-US">
             <span lang="EN-US">
              PYMCA
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </a>
          <span lang="EN-US">
           <span lang="EN-US">
            .
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2010/november/streetstyle_book_new_edition#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2010/november/streetstyle_book_new_edition">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2010/november/kings_of_leon_in_new_york_for_nme">
         Kings of Leon- in New York for NME
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        25 November 10
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  8:16
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TO6LxLvhO_I/AAAAAAAAAAk/kDN37SXEJA8/s1600/kol+cover.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="400" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TO6LxLvhO_I/AAAAAAAAAAk/kDN37SXEJA8/s400/kol+cover.jpg" width="317"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <div>
         Dean flew to New York to catch up with the Kings of Leon for the 21st August 2010 edition of the NME. The shoot took place at Milk Studios on Manhattan.
        </div>
        <p>
         The Kings were in fine spirits, it was the first shoot they had collectively done for a while
         <br/>
         <br/>
         The images accompanied an great interview by the journalist Barry Nicolson, in the wake of the incident (youll have to read more of the magazine to find out about that..). The article touches many issues that are close to the hearts of the band not least the subject of the bands reaction to being accused of selling out as well as offering a prelude to the bands eagerly anticipated 5th album Come Around Sundown.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         The shoot has a warm feel to it, Dean wanted to reflect the Followills homely small town, southern roots that challenges the Stadium Rock label that they have been attributed since the release of Because of the Times.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         According to those lucky enough to have had a sneak preview of the bands new record, it is reported to be very much back to their old roots, which will delight old fans as well as show the new comers the journey they have come.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         For more from this session go to NME.com or pop along to the news stand and pick up a copy of the magazine.
        </p>
       </div>
       <p class="comment_count">
        <a href="2010/november/kings_of_leon_in_new_york_for_nme#comments">
         <fb:comments-count href="http://www.deanchalkley.com/blog/2010/november/kings_of_leon_in_new_york_for_nme">
         </fb:comments-count>
         Comments
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>

         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>

        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
