           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           Dean met up with Tony Christie in the midst of his stint, treading the boards in the west-end musical show Dreamboats &amp; Petticoats
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
         <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           The shoot took place amidst the landmarks of Sohos old-school clubland, with scenes that would not have looked out of place in Colin MacInnes Absolute Beginners, Bar Italia and the rain splattered streets featured heavily.
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
         <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           Dean shot Tony for his brand new record Nows the Time, which is being released on Acid Jazz in January 2011.
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           The first single Nobody in the World out on the 8
          </span>
          <sup>
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            th
           </span>
          </sup>
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           November, has a great Northern Soul feel and would not be out of place in any self respecting soul DJs set.
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
         <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           Its the first release from Tony on the Acid Jazz label.
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           The Album Now is the Time, sees Christie, going back to his roots bringing together the sound of Northern Soul, British Beat and Cinematic sound-tracks.
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           Jarvis Cocker, a big fan of Tony, has reworked the iconic theme from the film Get Carter, for the album now entitled
          </span>
          <em>
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            Get Christie,
           </span>
          </em>
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           it has an additional classic line from the film hes a big man but hes out of shape nice touch.
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           More on the album as it approaches its release, but for the time being
          </span>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <a href="http://www.modculture.info/2010/09/tony-christie-turns-northern-soul.html">
           <span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             http://www.modculture.info/2010/09/tony-christie-turns-northern-soul.html
            </span>
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
          <br/>
         </span>
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span lang="EN-US">
          <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=etO9aPoy3hw">
           <span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">
            <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
             http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=etO9aPoy3hw
            </span>

           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            The hostess of Strictly Come Dancing was in a playful mood on the shoot and depicts Tess in a chic and glamorous way, far from the celebrity lifestyle magazines in which she is often portrayed. With elegant dresses by Stella McCartney and Amanda Wakeley and a hat by milliner Peter Betley.
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
         <div class="MsoNormal">
          <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
           <br/>
          </span>
         </div>
         <div class="MsoNormal">
          <span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 'Gill Sans';">
           <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-size: large;">
            The article by Elizabeth Day touches on the personal issues that have revolved around Tess life in the past year. In the article she also explains how her TV career took off and expresses her love for her dear friend, the late Quentin Crisp.
           </span>
          </span>

       <h2 class="title">
        <a href="2010/november/my_chemical_romance_nme_131110">
         My Chemical Romance - NME 13/11/10
        </a>
       </h2>
       <h3 class="date">
        13 November 10
       </h3>
       <h3 class="time">
        Posted at  9:30
       </h3>
       <div class="content">
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
         <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPUXhr2WPXI/AAAAAAAAABA/iEEQWjJkX5o/s1600/13NOV.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
          <img alt="" border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_6O8vTfG_cZM/TPUXhr2WPXI/AAAAAAAAABA/iEEQWjJkX5o/s640/13NOV.jpg" width="506"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
        </div>
        <div class="MsoNormal">
         <span lang="EN-US">
          Dean was asked by the NME to shoot My Chemical Romance last month. The results were published in the November 13
          <sup>
           th
          </sup>
          issue. The NME have used Gerard Way, with his striking new red hair as the cover shot.
         </span>
        </div>
       </div>

        js.src = '//connect.facebook.net/en_GB/sdk.js#xfbml=1&amp;version=v2.3';
        fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
      }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));
  </script>
